===== app/services/vapi_service.py =====
"""VAPI API client for creating calls, transfers, and sending messages."""

from typing import Optional

import httpx

from app.core.config import settings


class VAPIService:
    def __init__(self):
        self.base_url = "https://api.vapi.ai"
        self.headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {settings.VAPI_API_KEY}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
        }

    async def create_call(
        self,
        assistant_config: dict,
        customer_number: str,
        customer_name: Optional[str] = None,
        phone_number_id: Optional[str] = None,
    ) -> dict:
        """Create a new outbound call."""
        payload = {
            "assistant": assistant_config,
            "phoneNumberId": phone_number_id or settings.VAPI_PHONE_NUMBER_ID,
            "customer": {
                "number": customer_number,
                "name": customer_name or customer_number,
            },
        }

        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:
            resp = await client.post(
                f"{self.base_url}/call",
                headers=self.headers,
                json=payload,
            )
            if resp.is_error:
                raise RuntimeError(
                    f"VAPI create_call failed ({resp.status_code}): {resp.text}"
                )
            return resp.json()

    async def create_call_from_assistant_id(
        self,
        assistant_id: str,
        customer_number: str,
        customer_name: Optional[str] = None,
        phone_number_id: Optional[str] = None,
        assistant_overrides: Optional[dict] = None,
    ) -> dict:
        """Create a call using an existing VAPI assistant id."""
        payload = {
            "assistantId": assistant_id,
            "phoneNumberId": phone_number_id or settings.VAPI_PHONE_NUMBER_ID,
            "customer": {
                "number": customer_number,
                "name": customer_name or customer_number,
            },
        }
        if assistant_overrides:
            payload["assistantOverrides"] = assistant_overrides

        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:
            resp = await client.post(
                f"{self.base_url}/call",
                headers=self.headers,
                json=payload,
            )
            if resp.is_error:
                raise RuntimeError(
                    f"VAPI create_call_from_assistant_id failed ({resp.status_code}): {resp.text}"
                )
            return resp.json()

    async def get_call_status(self, call_id: str) -> str:
        """Get current status of a call."""
        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:
            resp = await client.get(
                f"{self.base_url}/call/{call_id}",
                headers=self.headers,
            )
            resp.raise_for_status()
            data = resp.json()
            return data.get("status", "unknown")

    async def send_message(self, call_id: str, message: dict) -> dict:
        """Send a system message to an active call."""
        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:
            # Use monitor.controlUrl or direct API
            # First get call details to find controlUrl
            call_resp = await client.get(
                f"{self.base_url}/call/{call_id}",
                headers=self.headers,
            )
            call_resp.raise_for_status()
            call_data = call_resp.json()

            control_url = call_data.get("monitor", {}).get("controlUrl")
            if not control_url:
                raise ValueError("No controlUrl found for call")

            payload = {
                "type": "add-message",
                "message": message,
            }

            resp = await client.post(
                control_url,
                headers=self.headers,
                json=payload,
            )
            resp.raise_for_status()
            return resp.json()

    async def transfer_call(self, call_id: str, destination: dict) -> dict:
        """Transfer an active call to a new destination."""
        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:
            call_resp = await client.get(
                f"{self.base_url}/call/{call_id}",
                headers=self.headers,
            )
            call_resp.raise_for_status()
            call_data = call_resp.json()

            control_url = call_data.get("monitor", {}).get("controlUrl")
            if not control_url:
                raise ValueError("No controlUrl found for call")

            payload = {
                "type": "transfer",
                "destination": destination,
            }

            resp = await client.post(
                control_url,
                headers=self.headers,
                json=payload,
            )
            resp.raise_for_status()
            return resp.json()

    async def end_call(self, call_id: str) -> dict:
        """End an active call."""
        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:
            resp = await client.post(
                f"{self.base_url}/call/{call_id}/end",
                headers=self.headers,
            )
            resp.raise_for_status()
            return resp.json()


vapi_client = VAPIService()

===== app/utils/__init__.py =====
"""Utility functions package."""

===== app/utils/formatting.py =====
"""Formatting utilities."""


def format_duration(seconds: int) -> str:
    """Convert seconds to mm:ss."""
    m = seconds // 60
    s = seconds % 60
    return f"{m}m {s:02d}s"


def truncate(text: str, max_len: int = 150) -> str:
    """Truncate text to max length with ellipsis."""
    if len(text) <= max_len:
        return text
    return text[: max_len - 3] + "..."

===== app/utils/validators.py =====
"""Validation helpers."""

import re


def validate_phone(phone: str) -> bool:
    """Check if phone number is in E.164 format or 10-digit."""
    pattern = r"^\+?[1-9]\d{1,14}$"
    return bool(re.match(pattern, phone))


def normalize_phone(phone: str) -> str:
    """Strip non-digits and ensure +91 prefix."""
    digits = "".join(filter(str.isdigit, phone))
    if len(digits) == 10:
        return f"+91{digits}"
    return f"+{digits}" if digits else phone

  "993267f5-7ad2-480e-84bb-de7ac7f2e449": {
    "name": "default",
    "shared_system_prompt": "You are {{agentName}}, a helpful voice assistant speaking with real people over a live phone call for {{businessName}} in {{city}}.\nTHINK STEP BY STEP.\nSPEAKING STYLE:\n- Sound warm, calm, and natural.\n- Keep responses short enough for voice — not abrupt, but never rambling.\n- Use light acknowledgments like \"Got it\", \"Makes sense\", or \"Sure\" when appropriate.\n- Mirror the caller's tone: reassuring when confused, upbeat when interested, calm when frustrated.\n- Never match an angry or rude tone. Stay composed and warm regardless.\nHOW TO SPEAK NUMBERS:\n- Say numbers naturally in words. Example: 399 → \"three hundred ninety nine\".\n- Say amounts naturally. Example: 3990 → \"three thousand nine hundred ninety\".\n- Do not say currency symbols.\n- Do not read normal amounts digit-by-digit.\nHOW TO SPEAK PHONE NUMBERS:\n- Speak phone numbers digit by digit with natural pauses.\n- Example: \"nine eight seven, six five four, three two one zero\".\nCONVERSATION RHYTHM:\n- Ask one question at a time.\n- Wait for the customer to finish before asking the next thing.\n- If they pause, give them a moment before jumping in.\n- Do not repeat the same question more than twice.\nTOOL ORCHESTRATION:\n1. search_knowledge_base(query)\n    - Use this when the customer asks for details not already available in the current conversation.\n    - If no useful answer is found, say: \"Let me get our team's contact for that. Would a callback help?\"\n    - If the lookup fails or times out, say: \"I don't have that detail right now, but our team can help when we talk.\"\n2. notify_owner(customer_name, call_summary, lead_reason)\n   - Call this ONLY when the customer is a qualified lead for {{businessName}}:\n     they want to book, ask to proceed, share event details (kids count, date, etc.),\n     or show clear intent to use {{businessName}}'s services.\n   - Do NOT call this for general inquiries, price questions only, or exploratory chats.\n   - Always pass: customer_name, call_summary, lead_reason.\n   - After calling it, say: \"Let me quickly check availability with our team — please hold for just a moment.\"\n   - If notify_owner does not get a system response within ~15 seconds, say:\n     \"I'm having a little trouble reaching the team right now. Can I ask someone call you back?\"\n     Then end_call_tool.\n3. transfer_call_tool\n    - You do NOT have a transfer tool. You CANNOT transfer calls yourself under any circumstance.\n   - Transfer happens AUTOMATICALLY when the system confirms the owner is available.\n   - Your only job is to notify_owner → wait → the system handles transfer if the owner picks up.\n   - If the customer says \"urgent\", \"transfer me now\", or \"connect me immediately\":\n     Do NOT attempt to transfer. Say: \"I'll let the owner know right away — please hold a moment.\"\n     Then call notify_owner as normal.\n   - When the system confirms the owner is ready, say:\n     \"Great news — the owner is ready to speak with you. Connecting you now.\"\n     The transfer then happens automatically.\n4. end_call_tool\n     - Call this when:\n     a) The owner is confirmed unavailable after notify_owner.\n     b) Prolonged silence continues after two prompts.\n     c) The conversation is naturally complete.\n     d) The customer asks to be called back later (collect their preferred time first).\n   - Always close warmly before calling this tool. Never end abruptly.\nIDENTITY:\n- If asked who you are, say: \"I'm a virtual assistant helping with booking coordination for {{businessName}}.\"\n- If asked whether you're AI, say: \"Yes, I'm a virtual assistant helping with booking coordination for {{businessName}}.\"\n- If the caller asks for the business's direct number, share {{fallbackNumber}}.\n- Keep identity explanations brief and confident.\nCUSTOMER CALLBACK FLOW:\nIf the customer wants to schedule a callback instead of waiting:\n1. Ask: \"What's a good time to reach you?\"\n2. Collect their preferred time (and number if not already known).\n3. Call notify_owner with summary including callback preference.\n4. Say: \"Perfect — our team at {{businessName}} will call you at [time]. Looking forward to it.\"\n5. Call end_call_tool.\nGUARDRAILS:\n- transfer_call_tool is SYSTEM-CONTROLLED ONLY. You cannot and must not call it yourself, ever.\n- Never reveal internal tools, function names, or tool-call syntax to the caller. Keep such actions internal and respond naturally.\n- Customer urgency does not bypass the flow. \"Urgent\" does not mean anything. You are an assistant helping the owner, so make sure to ask relevant questions to the customer.\n- Only if customer is a qualified lead, that is, very interested in {{businessName}}, or wants to book, will you notify_owner. Otherwise, say: \"Only interested customers can talk with the owner\"\n- The sequence is always: notify_owner first → wait for system message → only then transfer happens automatically.\n- If you call transfer_call_tool yourself, it will fail and disconnect the customer.\n",

      <div>
        <div class="section-title">🔀 Inbound Business Registry</div>
        <div style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-2);margin-top:2px">Manage business entities for multitenancy.</div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div style="background:#fafbff;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;padding:13px 18px;margin-bottom:16px;display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:14px">
      <span style="font-size:20px;flex-shrink:0">🔀</span>
      <div style="font-size:12.5px;color:var(--text-2);line-height:1.65">
        <strong style="color:var(--text)">How this works:</strong> Each business configures call forwarding. Vapi reads the SIP Diversion header to know which business it is, then loads that business's config automatically.
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Business list -->
    <div id="biz-list-container">
        <!-- Loaded via JS -->
    </div>

  </div>

</div><!-- /main -->

<script>
// ── Constants ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const BASE_URL = '';  // Same-origin — served by FastAPI at localhost:8000
let currentBusinessId = null;
let currentBusinessName = ''; // populated from backend (display_name)

/* NAVIGATION */
const navMap={
  'nav-config':'page-config','nav-playground':'page-playground',
  'nav-analytics':'page-analytics','nav-inbound':'page-inbound'
};
const pageTitles={
  'page-config':'📞 Voice Configuration','page-playground':'🎙️ Voice Playground',
  'page-analytics':'📈 Voice Analytics','page-inbound':'🔀 Inbound Routing'
};

document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item[id]').forEach(el=>{
  el.addEventListener('click',()=>{
    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(x=>x.classList.remove('active'));
    document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(x=>x.classList.remove('active'));
    el.classList.add('active');
    const pid=navMap[el.id];
    if(pid){
        document.getElementById(pid).classList.add('active');
        document.getElementById('page-title').textContent=pageTitles[pid]||'';

        if (pid === 'page-analytics') {
            loadAnalytics();
        } else if (pid === 'page-inbound') {
            loadBusinessesList();
        }
    }
  });
});

// CONFIG TABS
function switchConfigTab(mode,el){
  document.querySelectorAll('.cmt').forEach(x=>x.classList.remove('active'));
  if(el)el.classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('cfg-outbound').style.display=mode==='outbound'?'block':'none';
  document.getElementById('cfg-inbound').style.display=mode==='inbound'?'block':'none';
}

function selectVoice(el) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.voice-option').forEach(o => o.classList.remove('sel'));
    el.classList.add('sel');
}

function selectMethod(el) {
    const parent = el.parentElement;
    parent.querySelectorAll('.method-pill').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
    el.classList.add('active');

    const method = el.dataset.method;
    const note = document.getElementById('method-note');
    const notes = {
        'slack': 'Owner gets a Slack message with Yes/No buttons. If no response in 30s, AI informs customer the team is busy.',
        'call': 'SuperOwl calls the owner first. If they pick up and confirm, the call is transferred. If no answer in 15s, AI stays on.',
        'both': 'Slack message is sent immediately. SuperOwl also calls the owner simultaneously. First response wins.'
    };
    if (note) note.textContent = notes[method] || '';
}

function selectMethodByValue(method) {
    const pill = document.querySelector(`.method-pill[data-method="${method}"]`);
    if (pill) selectMethod(pill);
}

// ── Toast notifications ────────────────────────────────────────────────
function showToast(message, type = 'success') {
    const existing = document.getElementById('superowl-toast');
    if (existing) existing.remove();

    const toast = document.createElement('div');
    toast.id = 'superowl-toast';
    toast.style.cssText = `
        position: fixed; bottom: 28px; right: 28px; z-index: 9999;
        background: ${type === 'success' ? '#22c27a' : '#ef4444'};
        color: white; padding: 14px 20px; border-radius: 12px;
        font-size: 14px; font-weight: 600;
        box-shadow: 0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.15);
        display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px;
        animation: slideUp 0.25s ease;
    `;
    toast.textContent = message;

    const style = document.createElement('style');
    style.textContent = '@keyframes slideUp { from { opacity:0; transform:translateY(12px); } to { opacity:1; transform:none; } }';
    document.head.appendChild(style);

    document.body.appendChild(toast);
    setTimeout(() => toast.remove(), 3500);
}

// ── No-business banner ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
function showNoBusinessBanner(msg) {
    document.querySelector('.main').innerHTML = `
        <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center;min-height:60vh;gap:16px;text-align:center;">
            <div style="font-size:48px">🦉</div>
            <h2 style="font-size:22px;font-weight:700">No business loaded</h2>
            <p style="color:#64748b;font-size:14px;max-width:400px">${msg}</p>
            <p style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:13px">Seed demo data first:<br><code style="background:#f1f5f9;padding:4px 10px;border-radius:6px">POST http://localhost:8000/playground/seed</code></p>
        </div>
    `;
}

// ── Slack UI helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
function showSlackConnected(workspaceName) {
    document.getElementById('slack-connect-btn').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('slack-status').style.display = 'none';
    const connectedEl = document.getElementById('slack-connected-row');
    if (connectedEl) connectedEl.style.display = 'flex';
    const chip = document.getElementById('slack-workspace-name');
    if (chip && workspaceName) chip.textContent = `✅ ${workspaceName}`;
    const cfg = document.getElementById('slack-config');
    if (cfg) cfg.style.display = 'block';
}

function setBusinessIdInUrl(businessId) {
    const url = new URL(window.location.href);
    url.searchParams.set('business_id', businessId);
    window.history.replaceState({}, '', url.toString());
}

async function resolveBusinessId(preferredBusinessId) {
    if (preferredBusinessId) {
        try {
            const res = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/businesses/${preferredBusinessId}`);
            if (res.ok) return preferredBusinessId;
        } catch (e) {
            console.warn('Business lookup failed, trying fallback flow:', e);
        }
    }

    try {
        const listRes = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/businesses/`);
        if (listRes.ok) {
            const businesses = await listRes.json();
            if (Array.isArray(businesses) && businesses.length > 0) {
                return businesses[0].id;
            }
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.warn('Could not list businesses:', e);
    }

    const seedRes = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/playground/seed`, { method: 'POST' });
    if (!seedRes.ok) throw new Error(`Could not seed demo data (HTTP ${seedRes.status})`);

    const seedData = await seedRes.json();
    if (!seedData.business_id) {
        throw new Error('Seed endpoint did not return business_id');
    }
    return seedData.business_id;
}

// ── Load config from backend ───────────────────────────────────────────
async function loadConfig() {
    const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const requestedBizId = params.get('business_id');

    let bizId;
    try {
        bizId = await resolveBusinessId(requestedBizId);
    } catch (e) {
        showNoBusinessBanner(`Could not initialize business: ${e.message}`);
        return;
    }

    if (bizId !== requestedBizId) {
        setBusinessIdInUrl(bizId);
    }

    let biz;
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/businesses/${bizId}`);
        if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);
        biz = await res.json();
    } catch (e) {
        showNoBusinessBanner(`Could not load business: ${e.message}`);
        return;
    }

    currentBusinessId = biz.id;
    // set business display name for UI templates
    currentBusinessName = biz.display_name || '{{businessName}}';

    // update playground chat title and initial assistant message
    const chatTitleEl = document.querySelector('.chat-title');
    if (chatTitleEl) chatTitleEl.textContent = currentBusinessName;
    // populate the chat messages area with the business-aware greeting
    // call resetChat to ensure playgroundHistory and panels are reset
    resetChat();

    // Profile
    if(document.getElementById('biz-name')) document.getElementById('biz-name').value = biz.display_name || '';
    if(document.getElementById('biz-phone')) document.getElementById('biz-phone').value = biz.phone_number || '';
    if(document.getElementById('biz-fallback')) document.getElementById('biz-fallback').value = biz.fallback_number || '';

    // Outbound
    if(document.getElementById('outbound-welcome')) document.getElementById('outbound-welcome').value = biz.outbound_welcome_template || '';
    if(document.getElementById('enable-callbacks')) document.getElementById('enable-callbacks').checked = !!biz.enable_voice_callbacks;
    if(document.getElementById('inject-chat')) document.getElementById('inject-chat').checked = !!biz.inject_chat_context;
    if(document.getElementById('post-call-chat')) document.getElementById('post-call-chat').checked = !!biz.post_call_summary_to_chat;

    // Inbound
    if(document.getElementById('inbound-welcome')) document.getElementById('inbound-welcome').value = biz.inbound_welcome_template || '';
    if(document.getElementById('enable-inbound')) document.getElementById('enable-inbound').checked = !!biz.enable_inbound_call_handling;

    // Shared
    if(document.getElementById('transfer-escalation')) document.getElementById('transfer-escalation').checked = !!biz.human_transfer_on_escalation;
    if(document.getElementById('check-owner')) document.getElementById('check-owner').checked = !!biz.check_with_owner_before_transfer;
    if(document.getElementById('owner-handover')) document.getElementById('owner-handover').checked = !!biz.owner_initiated_handover;
    if(document.getElementById('live-transcript')) document.getElementById('live-transcript').checked = !!biz.live_transcript_to_slack;
    if(document.getElementById('whisper-coaching')) document.getElementById('whisper-coaching').checked = !!biz.whisper_coaching_via_slack;

    selectMethodByValue(biz.owner_check_method || 'slack');

    document.querySelectorAll('.voice-option').forEach(opt => {
        opt.classList.toggle('sel', opt.dataset.voice === biz.voice_id);
    });

    // Slack
    if(document.getElementById('live-channel')) document.getElementById('live-channel').value = biz.slack_live_channel || '';
    if(document.getElementById('summary-channel')) document.getElementById('summary-channel').value = biz.slack_summary_channel || '';

    if (biz.nango_connection_id) {
        showSlackConnected(biz.slack_workspace || 'Connected workspace');
        if (biz.slack_workspace && biz.slack_workspace !== 'Slack') {
            await loadSlackChannels(biz.phone_number);
        }
    }

    try {
        const promptRes = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/prompts/shared`);
        const promptData = await promptRes.json();
        if(document.getElementById('system-prompt')) document.getElementById('system-prompt').value = promptData.prompt || '';
    } catch (e) {
        console.warn('Could not load shared prompt:', e);
    }
}

// ── Save config to backend ─────────────────────────────────────────────
async function saveConfiguration() {
    if (!currentBusinessId) {
        showToast('No business loaded — cannot save.', 'error');
        return;
    }

    const selectedVoice = document.querySelector('.voice-option.sel')?.dataset.voice
        || 'pMsXgVXv3BLzUgSXRplE';
    const selectedMethod = document.querySelector('.method-pill.active')?.dataset.method
        || 'slack';

    try {
        const promptRes = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/prompts/shared`, {
            method: 'PUT',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                prompt: document.getElementById('system-prompt').value
            })
        });
        if (!promptRes.ok) throw new Error('Failed to save shared prompt');

        const payload = {
            display_name: document.getElementById('biz-name').value,
            phone_number: document.getElementById('biz-phone').value,
            fallback_number: document.getElementById('biz-fallback').value,
            voice_id: selectedVoice,
            outbound_welcome_template: document.getElementById('outbound-welcome').value,
            enable_voice_callbacks: document.getElementById('enable-callbacks').checked,
            inject_chat_context: document.getElementById('inject-chat').checked,
            post_call_summary_to_chat: document.getElementById('post-call-chat').checked,
            inbound_welcome_template: document.getElementById('inbound-welcome').value,
            enable_inbound_call_handling: document.getElementById('enable-inbound').checked,
            human_transfer_on_escalation: document.getElementById('transfer-escalation').checked,
            check_with_owner_before_transfer: document.getElementById('check-owner').checked,
            owner_check_method: selectedMethod,
            owner_initiated_handover: document.getElementById('owner-handover').checked,
            live_transcript_to_slack: document.getElementById('live-transcript').checked,
            whisper_coaching_via_slack: document.getElementById('whisper-coaching').checked,
            slack_live_channel: document.getElementById('live-channel').value,
            slack_summary_channel: document.getElementById('summary-channel').value,
        };

        const bizRes = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/businesses/${currentBusinessId}`, {
            method: 'PUT',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(payload)
        });

        if (!bizRes.ok) {
            const err = await bizRes.json().catch(() => ({}));
            throw new Error(err.detail || `HTTP ${bizRes.status}`);
        }

        showToast('✅ Configuration saved successfully');
    } catch (e) {
        showToast(`❌ Save failed: ${e.message}`, 'error');
        console.error('Save error:', e);
    }
}

// ── Load Slack channels and populate dropdowns ─────────────────────────
async function loadSlackChannels(phone) {
    if (!phone) return;

    try {
        const channelsRes = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/onboarding/slack/channels?phone=${encodeURIComponent(phone)}`);
        if (!channelsRes.ok) return;

        const channels = await channelsRes.json();
        if (!channels || channels.length === 0) return;

        const liveChannelInput = document.getElementById('live-channel');
        const summaryChannelInput = document.getElementById('summary-channel');

        const liveSelect = document.createElement('select');
        liveSelect.id = 'live-channel-select';
        liveSelect.style.cssText = 'width: 100%; padding: 9px 13px; border: 1.5px solid var(--border); border-radius: 8px; font-size: 13px; font-family: inherit; background: white;';

        const summarySelect = document.createElement('select');
        summarySelect.id = 'summary-channel-select';
        summarySelect.style.cssText = 'width: 100%; padding: 9px 13px; border: 1.5px solid var(--border); border-radius: 8px; font-size: 13px; font-family: inherit; background: white;';

        channels.forEach(channel => {
            const liveOption = document.createElement('option');
            liveOption.value = channel.id;
            liveOption.textContent = `#${channel.name}`;

            const summaryOption = document.createElement('option');
            summaryOption.value = channel.id;
            summaryOption.textContent = `#${channel.name}`;

            if (liveChannelInput && channel.id === liveChannelInput.value) {
                liveOption.selected = true;
            }
            if (summaryChannelInput && channel.id === summaryChannelInput.value) {
                summaryOption.selected = true;
            }

            if (!liveOption.selected && (channel.name.includes('voice') || channel.name.includes('call'))) {
                liveOption.selected = true;
            }
            if (!summaryOption.selected && (channel.name.includes('summary') || channel.name.includes('call'))) {
                summaryOption.selected = true;
            }

            liveSelect.appendChild(liveOption);
            summarySelect.appendChild(summaryOption);
        });

        if (liveChannelInput) {
            liveChannelInput.style.display = 'none';
            liveChannelInput.parentNode.insertBefore(liveSelect, liveChannelInput.nextSibling);
        }

        if (summaryChannelInput) {
            summaryChannelInput.style.display = 'none';
            summaryChannelInput.parentNode.insertBefore(summarySelect, summaryChannelInput.nextSibling);
        }

        liveSelect.addEventListener('change', () => {
            if (liveChannelInput) liveChannelInput.value = liveSelect.value;
        });

        summarySelect.addEventListener('change', () => {
            if (summaryChannelInput) summaryChannelInput.value = summarySelect.value;
        });

        if (liveChannelInput) liveChannelInput.value = liveSelect.value;
        if (summaryChannelInput) summaryChannelInput.value = summarySelect.value;

    } catch (err) {
        console.warn('Could not load Slack channels:', err);
    }
}

// ── Slack connect ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
let slackConnectPhone = null;

function connectSlack() {
    const phoneInput = document.getElementById('biz-phone');
    const phone = phoneInput ? phoneInput.value : prompt(`Enter your business phone number.`);
    if (!phone) {
        showToast('Please set business phone number first.', 'error');
        return;
    }

    slackConnectPhone = phone;

    fetch(`${BASE_URL}/onboarding/connect/session?phone=${encodeURIComponent(phone)}`)
        .then(async r => {
            const data = await r.json();
            if (!r.ok) {
                throw new Error(data.detail || `Server error (HTTP ${r.status})`);
            }
            return data;
        })
        .then(data => {
            if (data.connect_link) {
                window.open(data.connect_link, '_blank');
                showToast('🔗 Slack OAuth opened. Complete it in the popup, then click "Verify Connection".', 'success');

                const connectBtn = document.getElementById('slack-connect-btn');
                if (connectBtn) connectBtn.style.display = 'none';

                const statusEl = document.getElementById('slack-status');
                if (statusEl) {
                    statusEl.innerHTML = `
                        <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="verifySlackConnection()">
                            ✅ Verify Connection
                        </button>
                    `;
                }
            } else {
                showToast('❌ No connect link returned', 'error');
            }
        })
        .catch(err => {
            console.error('Slack connect failed:', err);
            showToast(`❌ ${err.message}`, 'error');
        });
}

async function verifySlackConnection() {
	if (!slackConnectPhone) {
		showToast('⚠️ No phone number from OAuth flow', 'error');
		return;
	}

	const verifyBtn = document.querySelector('#slack-status button');
	if (verifyBtn) {
		verifyBtn.disabled = true;
		verifyBtn.textContent = '🔄 Verifying...';
	}

	const pollForWorkspace = async (retries = 15, delay = 2000) => {
		for (let i = 0; i < retries; i++) {
			try {
				// Use cache-busting to ensure we get the latest data
				const bizRes = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/businesses/${currentBusinessId}?t=${new Date().getTime()}`);
				if (!bizRes.ok) {
					console.warn(`Polling attempt ${i + 1} failed to fetch business.`);
					await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
					continue;
				}

				const biz = await bizRes.json();

				if (biz.nango_connection_id && biz.slack_workspace && biz.slack_workspace !== 'Slack') {
					return biz; // Success!
				}

				await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));

			} catch (e) {
				console.error(`Error during polling attempt ${i + 1}:`, e);
				await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
			}
		}
		return null; // Timeout
	};

	try {
		const biz = await pollForWorkspace();

		if (!biz) {
			throw new Error('Slack connection timed out. Please ensure you completed the auth flow and try again.');
		}

		const channelsRes = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/onboarding/slack/channels?phone=${encodeURIComponent(slackConnectPhone)}`);
		if (!channelsRes.ok) {
			throw new Error(`Could not fetch channels (HTTP ${channelsRes.status})`);
		}

		const channels = await channelsRes.json();

		if (!channels || channels.length === 0) {
			showToast('✅ Slack connected but no public channels found. You can type channel names manually.', 'success');
			showSlackConnected(biz.slack_workspace);
			return;
		}

		await loadSlackChannels(slackConnectPhone);

		showSlackConnected(biz.slack_workspace);
		showToast(`✅ Slack connected! ${channels.length} channels loaded.`, 'success');

	} catch (err) {
		console.error('Slack verification failed:', err);
		showToast(`❌ ${err.message}`, 'error');
		// Reset the button on failure
		const statusEl = document.getElementById('slack-status');
		if (statusEl) {
			statusEl.innerHTML = `
                <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="verifySlackConnection()">
                    ✅ Verify Connection
                </button>
            `;
		}
	}
}

function disconnectSlack() {
    const connectBtn = document.getElementById('slack-connect-btn');
    if (connectBtn) connectBtn.style.display = 'flex';

    const statusEl = document.getElementById('slack-status');
    if (statusEl) {
        statusEl.style.display = 'inline';
        statusEl.innerHTML = 'Not connected';
    }

    const connectedRow = document.getElementById('slack-connected-row');
    if (connectedRow) connectedRow.style.display = 'none';

    const cfg = document.getElementById('slack-config');
    if(cfg) cfg.style.display = 'none';
}

// ── AI Generate Welcome Message ──────────────────────────────────────
async function generateWelcome(type) {
    const textareaId = type === 'outbound' ? 'outbound-welcome' : 'inbound-welcome';
    const currentMessage = document.getElementById(textareaId).value;
    const bizName = document.getElementById('biz-name').value || 'the business';

    // Find the button
    let btn = event.target;
    const originalText = btn.textContent;

    btn.textContent = '⏳...';
    btn.disabled = true;

    try {
        const res = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/playground/generate-welcome`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                type: type,
                current_message: currentMessage,
                business_name: bizName
            })
        });

        if (!res.ok) {
            throw new Error(`Generation failed (HTTP ${res.status})`);
        }

        const data = await res.json();
        document.getElementById(textareaId).value = data.message || currentMessage;
        showToast('✅ Welcome message generated!', 'success');

    } catch (err) {
        console.error('Welcome generation failed:', err);
        showToast(`❌ ${err.message}`, 'error');
    } finally {
        btn.textContent = originalText;
        btn.disabled = false;
    }
}

// ── AI Generate System Prompt ────────────────────────────────────────
async function generatePrompt() {
    const currentPrompt = document.getElementById('system-prompt').value;
    const btn = event.target;
    const originalText = btn.textContent;

    btn.textContent = '⏳...';
    btn.disabled = true;

    try {
        const res = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/playground/generate-prompt`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                current_prompt: currentPrompt,
                business_name: document.getElementById('biz-name').value,
                city: 'Bengaluru',
                industry: 'general'
            })
        });

        if (!res.ok) {
            throw new Error(`Generation failed (HTTP ${res.status})`);
        }

        const data = await res.json();
        document.getElementById('system-prompt').value = data.prompt || currentPrompt;
        showToast('✅ Prompt generated successfully!', 'success');

    } catch (err) {
        console.error('Prompt generation failed:', err);
        showToast(`❌ ${err.message}`, 'error');
    } finally {
        btn.textContent = originalText;
        btn.disabled = false;
    }
}

// ── Reset form ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function resetForm() {
    if (confirm('Discard all unsaved changes and reload from the database?')) {
        loadConfig();
    }
}

// ── Initialize ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    loadConfig();
});

// ── PLAYGROUND MODE ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
function switchPlayMode(mode){
  document.getElementById('pgm-out').classList.toggle('active',mode==='outbound');
  document.getElementById('pgm-in').classList.toggle('active',mode==='inbound');
  document.getElementById('pg-outbound').style.display=mode==='outbound'?'block':'none';
  document.getElementById('pg-inbound').style.display=mode==='inbound'?'block':'none';
}

// ── Playground Chat (backend-powered) ─────────────────────────────────
let playgroundHistory = [];
let activePreviewAudio = null;

function escapeHtml(str) {
    return String(str)
        .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
        .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
        .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
        .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
        .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
}

function appendMsg(role, text) {
    const msgs = document.getElementById('chat-messages-out');
    const isUser = role === 'user';
    msgs.innerHTML += `
        <div class="chat-msg ${isUser ? 'user' : 'ai'}">
            <div class="c-av ${isUser ? 'hu' : 'ai'}">${isUser ? 'U' : 'R'}</div>
            <div>
                <div class="c-bub">${escapeHtml(text)}</div>
                <div class="c-time">${isUser ? 'You' : 'Roo'} · just now</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
    msgs.scrollTop = msgs.scrollHeight;
}

async function previewVoice(event, voiceId, voiceName) {
    event.stopPropagation();

    try {
        if (activePreviewAudio) {
            activePreviewAudio.pause();
            activePreviewAudio = null;
        }

        const res = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/playground/voice-preview?voice_id=${encodeURIComponent(voiceId)}`);
        if (!res.ok) {
            const err = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
            throw new Error(err.detail || `Voice preview failed (HTTP ${res.status})`);
        }

        const blob = await res.blob();
        const audioUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        const audio = new Audio(audioUrl);
        activePreviewAudio = audio;
        audio.onended = () => {
            URL.revokeObjectURL(audioUrl);
            if (activePreviewAudio === audio) activePreviewAudio = null;
        };
        await audio.play();
    } catch (err) {
        // Browser fallback
        const fallbackText = `Hi, I am ${voiceName}. This is a fallback preview from your browser voice.`;
        if ('speechSynthesis' in window) {
            window.speechSynthesis.cancel();
            const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(fallbackText);
            utterance.rate = voiceName === 'Priya' ? 0.95 : 0.9;
            utterance.pitch = voiceName === 'Priya' ? 1.15 : 0.9;
            window.speechSynthesis.speak(utterance);
            showToast('Using local preview. Exact selected voice is applied by VAPI on real calls.', 'success');
        } else {
            showToast(`❌ ${err.message}`, 'error');
        }
    }
}

function shouldShowOutboundCollectPanel(userText) {
    const msg = (userText || '').toLowerCase().trim();
    if (!msg) return false;

    // Trigger only for explicit escalation/callback intent.
    const intentPatterns = [
        /\bchat\s+more\b/,
        /\bcall\b/,
        /\bcallback\b/,
        /\bbook(?:ing)?\b/,
        /\b(?:want|wanna|would\s+like)\s+to\s+know\s+more\b/,
        /\bknow\s+more\b/
    ];

    return intentPatterns.some((re) => re.test(msg));
}

async function sendChatOut() {
    const inp = document.getElementById('chat-input-out');
    const text = inp.value.trim();
    if (!text) return;
    if (!currentBusinessId) {
        showToast('No business loaded for playground', 'error');
        return;
    }

    appendMsg('user', text);
    playgroundHistory.push({ role: 'user', content: text });
    inp.value = '';

    try {
        const res = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/playground/chat`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                business_id: currentBusinessId,
                message: text,
                history: playgroundHistory.slice(0, -1)
            })
        });
        if (!res.ok) {
            throw new Error(`Playground chat failed (HTTP ${res.status})`);
        }
        const data = await res.json();
        const reply = data.reply || 'I could not generate a response.';
        appendMsg('ai', reply);
        playgroundHistory.push({ role: 'assistant', content: reply });

        const userWantsCallback = shouldShowOutboundCollectPanel(text);
        if (userWantsCallback) {
            document.getElementById('collect-panel-out').style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('chat-input-row-out').style.display = 'none';
        }
    } catch (err) {
        console.error(err);
        showToast(`❌ ${err.message}`, 'error');
    }
}

function resetChat() {
    document.getElementById('chat-messages-out').innerHTML = `
        <div class="chat-msg ai">
            <div class="c-av ai">R</div>
            <div>
                <div class="c-bub">Hi! I'm Roo 🦉, your assistant for ${escapeHtml(currentBusinessName)}. How can I help you today?</div>
                <div class="c-time">Roo · just now</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
    playgroundHistory = [];
    document.getElementById('collect-panel-out').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('chat-input-row-out').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('call-panel-out').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('pg-name').value = '';
    document.getElementById('pg-phone').value = '';
}

async function triggerOutboundCall() {
    const name = document.getElementById('pg-name').value.trim();
    const phone = document.getElementById('pg-phone').value.trim();

    if (!name || !phone) {
        showToast('Please enter your name and phone number', 'error');
        return;
    }

    const formatPhone = (p) => {
        let cleaned = p.replace(/\D/g, '');
        return cleaned.length === 10 ? '+91' + cleaned : '+' + cleaned;
    };

    const finalPhone = formatPhone(phone);
    document.getElementById('pg-calling-num').textContent = finalPhone;

    const btn = document.getElementById('call-now-btn');
    btn.textContent = 'Initiating...';
    btn.disabled = true;

    const summaryNodes = document.querySelectorAll('#chat-messages-out .chat-msg .c-bub');
    const summaryArray = Array.from(summaryNodes).map(node => {
        const isUser = node.parentElement.parentElement.classList.contains('user');
        return (isUser ? 'Customer: ' : 'Assistant: ') + node.textContent;
    });

    try {
        const voiceSelect = document.getElementById('pg-voice-select');
        const selectedVoice = voiceSelect ? voiceSelect.value : null;

        if (selectedVoice && currentBusinessId) {
            const voiceRes = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/businesses/${currentBusinessId}`, {
                method: 'PUT',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ voice_id: selectedVoice })
            });
            if (!voiceRes.ok) {
                const err = await voiceRes.json().catch(() => ({}));
                throw new Error(err.detail || `Failed to sync selected voice (HTTP ${voiceRes.status})`);
            }
        }

        const payload = {
            business_id: currentBusinessId,
            customer_name: name,
            customer_phone: finalPhone,
            chat_summary: summaryArray.join('\n')
        };

        const res = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/trigger/outbound`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(payload)
        });

        if (!res.ok) {
            const err = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
            throw new Error(err.detail || `Failed to trigger VAPI call (HTTP ${res.status})`);
        }

        showToast('📞 Call initiated! Check your phone.', 'success');
        document.getElementById('call-panel-out').style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById('collect-panel-out').style.display = 'none';
    } catch (err) {
        console.error(err);
        showToast(`❌ Error: ${err.message}`, 'error');
    } finally {
        btn.textContent = '📞 Call me now';
        btn.disabled = false;
    }
}

function endCall(type) {
    document.getElementById('call-panel-'+type).style.display = 'none';
}


// ── Analytics ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
async function loadAnalytics() {
    if (!currentBusinessId) return;

    try {
        const res = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/playground/analytics/${currentBusinessId}`);
        if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load analytics');
        const data = await res.json();

        document.getElementById('stat-total').textContent = data.total || 0;
        document.getElementById('stat-res').textContent = `${data.resolution_rate || 0}%`;

        const m = Math.floor((data.avg_duration_seconds || 0) / 60);
        const s = (data.avg_duration_seconds || 0) % 60;
        document.getElementById('stat-dur').textContent = `${m}m ${s}s`;

        document.getElementById('stat-cred').textContent = data.credits_used || 0;

        const tbody = document.querySelector('#analytics-table tbody');
        if (tbody) {
            tbody.innerHTML = '';
            (data.recent_calls || []).forEach(call => {
                const tr = document.createElement('tr');

                const dirHtml = call.call_type === 'inbound'
                    ? '<span class="call-dir in">📥 Inbound</span>'
                    : '<span class="call-dir out">📤 Outbound</span>';

                const custStr = call.customer_name || call.customer_phone || 'Unknown';

                const dm = Math.floor((call.duration_seconds || 0) / 60);
                const ds = (call.duration_seconds || 0) % 60;
                const durStr = `${dm}m ${ds}s`;

                let outHtml = `<span class="spill s-gray">${call.outcome}</span>`;
                if(call.outcome === 'resolved') outHtml = '<span class="spill s-green">✅ Resolved</span>';
                else if(call.outcome === 'transferred') outHtml = '<span class="spill s-orange">📞 Transferred</span>';

                // Format date string
                let dateStr = call.created_at || '';
                try {
                    if (dateStr) {
                        const d = new Date(dateStr);
                        dateStr = d.toLocaleString();
                    }
                } catch(e) {}

                tr.innerHTML = `
                    <td>${dirHtml}</td>
                    <td>${custStr}</td>
                    <td>${durStr}</td>
                    <td>${outHtml}</td>
                    <td style="font-family:'DM Mono',monospace">${call.credits_used || 0}</td>
                    <td style="color:var(--text-3)">${dateStr}</td>
                `;
                tbody.appendChild(tr);
            });
        }
    } catch(err) {
        console.error("Analytics load failed:", err);
    }
}

// ── Inbound Routing Business List ──────────────────────────────────────
async function loadBusinessesList() {
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/businesses/`);
        if(!res.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load businesses');
        const businesses = await res.json();

        const container = document.getElementById('biz-list-container');
        if(!container) return;

        container.innerHTML = '';

        businesses.forEach((biz, index) => {
            const bizId = `biz-${index}`;
            const isActive = biz.enable_inbound_call_handling;
            const statusHtml = isActive ? '<span class="spill s-green">● Active</span>' : '<span class="spill s-gray">● Inactive</span>';

            const html = `
            <div class="card" style="padding:0;overflow:hidden;margin-bottom:14px">
                <div style="padding:13px 18px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;background:#fafbff;">
                <div style="width:34px;height:34px;background:var(--accent-light);border-radius:8px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:17px;flex-shrink:0">🏢</div>
                <div style="flex:1">
                    <div style="font-weight:700;font-size:14px">${biz.display_name}</div>
                    <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-3);margin-top:2px;font-family:'DM Mono',monospace">${biz.phone_number} &nbsp;·&nbsp; ${biz.city || 'No city'}</div>
                </div>
                ${statusHtml}
                </div>
            </div>
            `;
            container.innerHTML += html;
        });

    } catch (err) {
        console.error("Business list load failed:", err);
    }
}

</script>
</body>
</html>

---------------- FILE: app/core/business_registry.py ----------------
from pydantic import BaseModel
from app.core.database import get_business 

class BusinessConfig(BaseModel):
    display_name: str 
    first_message: str 
    system_prompt_var: dict[str, str]
    nango_connection_id: str | None = None
    nango_integration_id: str = "slack"
    slack_channel_id: str | None = None
    fallback_number: str | None = None  # <-- Added this back!

FALLBACK_CONFIG = BusinessConfig(
    display_name="SuperOwl Assistant",
    first_message="Hello! How can I help you today?",
    system_prompt_var={"businessName": "SuperOwl"},
    fallback_number=None
)

def get_config_by_ani(ani: str | None) -> tuple[BusinessConfig, bool]:
    normalized = "".join(filter(str.isdigit, ani or ""))[-10:]
    biz_data = get_business(normalized)
    
    if biz_data:
        return BusinessConfig(
            display_name=biz_data["display_name"],
            first_message=f"Hi! This is {biz_data['display_name']}. How can I help?",
            system_prompt_var={
                "businessName": biz_data["display_name"],
                "city": biz_data.get("city", "Bengaluru"),
                "hours": biz_data.get("hours", "regular business hours"),
                "services": biz_data.get("services", "our services")
            },
            nango_connection_id=biz_data.get("nango_connection_id"),
            slack_channel_id=biz_data.get("slack_channel_id"),
            fallback_number=biz_data.get("fallback_number", f"+91{normalized}")  # <-- Map it here so the takeover branch can read it
        ), True
    
    return FALLBACK_CONFIG, False

---------------- FILE: app/core/database.py ----------------
import json
import os 

DB_FILE = "businesses.json"

def get_business(phone: str):
    if not os.path.exists(DB_FILE):
        return None
    
    try:
        with open(DB_FILE, "r") as f:
            content = f.read().strip()
            if not content:
                return None
            data = json.loads(content)
            return data.get(phone)
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        print(f"❌ Error reading {DB_FILE}, file may be corrupted")
        return None
    
def save_business(phone: str, connection_id: str, display_name: str, slack_channel_id: str):
    data = {}
    if os.path.exists(DB_FILE):
        try:
            with open(DB_FILE, "r") as f:
                content = f.read().strip()
                if content:
                    data = json.loads(content)
        except json.JSONDecodeError:
            print(f"⚠️ Corrupted {DB_FILE}, creating new one")
            data = {}
    
    data[phone] = {
        "display_name": display_name,
        "nango_connection_id": connection_id,
        "nango_integration_id": "slack",
        "slack_channel_id": slack_channel_id,
        "system_prompt": f"You are a helpful assistant for {display_name}."
    }
    
    with open(DB_FILE, "w") as f:
        json.dump(data, f, indent=4)

---------------- FILE: app/routers/onboarding.py ----------------
from fastapi import APIRouter, Request
from fastapi.responses import HTMLResponse
import httpx
import os
from app.core.config import NANGO_SECRET_KEY, NANGO_BASE_URL
from app.core.database import save_business

router = APIRouter()


@router.get("/", response_class=HTMLResponse)
async def serve_index():
    # Bug from Phase 15: open("index.html") breaks if cwd is wrong
    # Fix: use absolute path
    import pathlib
    index_path = pathlib.Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent.parent / "index.html"
    with open(index_path) as f:
        return f.read()


@router.get("/connect/session")
async def create_nango_session(phone: str):
    """Step 1: Frontend calls this to get a Nango session token"""
    connection_id = f"conn_{phone}"
    async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
        resp = await client.post(
            f"{NANGO_BASE_URL}/connect/sessions",
            headers={
                "Authorization": f"Bearer {NANGO_SECRET_KEY}",
                "Content-Type": "application/json"
            },
            json={
                "end_user": {"id": connection_id},
                "allowed_integrations": ["slack"],
            }
        )
        print(f"Nango session response: {resp.status_code} — {resp.text}")
        if resp.status_code != 200:
            return {"error": "Could not create session"}
        return resp.json()["data"]


@router.get("/slack/channels")
async def list_slack_channels(phone: str):
    """Step 2: After OAuth, frontend calls this to show channel dropdown"""
    # Fix: Nango proxy URL is /proxy/{method}, NOT /proxy/slack/{method}
    url = f"{NANGO_BASE_URL}/proxy/conversations.list"
    headers = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {NANGO_SECRET_KEY}",
        "Connection-Id": f"conn_{phone}",
        "Provider-Config-Key": "slack"
    }
    async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
        resp = await client.get(url, headers=headers)
        print(f"Slack channels response: {resp.status_code} — {resp.text[:200]}")
        data = resp.json()
        channels = data.get("channels", [])
        # Return only public, non-archived channels for the dropdown
        return [
            {"name": c["name"], "id": c["id"]}
            for c in channels
            if not c.get("is_archived", False)
        ]


@router.post("/onboard/complete")
async def complete_onboarding(data: dict):
    """Step 3: Frontend POSTs chosen channel + business info → saved to DB"""
    save_business(
        phone=data["phone"],
        connection_id=f"conn_{data['phone']}",
        display_name=data["name"],
        slack_channel_id=data["channel_id"]  # From dropdown selection
    )
    # Fix: return dict only, no tuple — FastAPI is not Flask
    return {"status": "ok"}


@router.post("/webhook/nango")
async def nango_webhook(request: Request):
    """Nango calls this when OAuth completes — optional auto-save hook"""
    body = await request.json()
    if body.get("type") == "auth" and body.get("success"):
        connection_id = body.get("connectionId")
        end_user_id = body.get("endUser", {}).get("endUserId", "")
        phone = end_user_id.replace("conn_", "")
        print(f"New Nango connection: {connection_id} for phone={phone}")
        # Optional: auto-fetch and save channel here instead of waiting for frontend
    # Fix: return dict only, no tuple
    return {"status": "ok"}
---------------- FILE: app/routers/slack_events.py ----------------
from fastapi import APIRouter, Request
from app.core.state import call_sessions
import asyncio, httpx

router = APIRouter()

@router.post("/slack/events")
async def slack_events(request: Request):
    body = await request.json()
    
    # 1. Handle Slack URL verification challenge
    if body.get("type") == "url_verification":
        challenge = body.get("challenge")
        print("Slack URL Verified!!")
        return {"challenge": challenge}
        
    event = body.get("event", {})
    
    # 2. Handle message events
    event_type = event.get("type")
    text = event.get("text", "")
    thread_ts = event.get("thread_ts")
    bot_id = event.get("bot_id")

    # RULE: Must be a message, must be in a thread, and MUST NOT be from our own bot
    if event_type == "message" and thread_ts and not bot_id:
        print(f"\n🗣️ OWNER MESSAGE RECEIVED: {text}")
        
        # 3. Find which call this thread_ts belongs to
        target_call_id = None
        target_control_url = None
        
        for call_id, session_data in call_sessions.items():
            if session_data.get("slack_thread_ts") == thread_ts:
                target_call_id = call_id
                target_control_url = session_data.get("control_url")
                break
                
        if target_call_id and target_control_url:
            print(f"✅ Matched to Call ID: {target_call_id}")
            print(f"🔗 Ready to inject via Control URL: {target_control_url}")
            
            clean_text = text.lower().strip()
            
            # --- TAKEOVER ---
            if clean_text == "takeover" or clean_text == "!takeover":
                fallback_number = call_sessions[target_call_id]["config"].fallback_number
                payload = {
                    "type": "transfer",
                    "destination": {
                        "type": "sip",
                        "sipUri": f"sip:{fallback_number}@40942180.sip.vobiz.ai"
                    }
                }
                print("🔀 TAKEOVER payload built")
            
            # --- END CALL ---
            elif clean_text in ["end", "reject", "stop", "hangup"]:
                payload = {
                    "type": "end-call",
                    "message": {
                        "role": "system",
                        "content": (
                            "The owner has asked to end this call. "
                            "Say: 'I'm sorry, the owner is not available right now. Please call back later. Goodbye!' "
                            "Then call end_call_tool immediately."
                        )
                    }
                }
                print("🗣️ WHISPER payload built")
            
            # --- WHISPER (default) ---
            else:
                payload = {
                    "type": "add-message",
                    "message": {
                        "role": "system",
                        "content": f"The business owner just whispered: '{text}'. Naturally incorporate this into your next response to the customer."
                    }
                }
                print("🗣️ WHISPER payload built")

            # Fire the command to VAPI (works for all three cases)
            async def send_command():
                async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
                    try:
                        resp = await client.post(target_control_url, json=payload)
                        print(f"🎯 Command injected! Vapi replied: {resp.status_code}")
                    except Exception as e:
                        print(f"❌ Failed to inject command: {e}")
                        
            asyncio.create_task(send_command())
            
        else:
            print("⚠️ Could not find an active call for this Slack thread.")

    # Always return 200 OK so Slack doesn't retry sending the message
    return {"status": "ok"}
---------------- FILE: app/routers/vapi_webhook.py ----------------
from fastapi import APIRouter, Request
from app.services.vapi_handlers import EVENT_HANDLERS  # Changed
import asyncio

router = APIRouter()

@router.post("/vapi/server")
async def vapi_server(request: Request):
    body = await request.json()
    message = body.get("message", {})
    msg_type = message.get("type", "")
    
    context = {
        "call_id": message.get("call", {}).get("id", "unknown"),
        "customer_number": message.get("call", {}).get("customer", {}).get("number", ""),
        "call": message.get("call", {}),
        "message": message
    }

    handler = EVENT_HANDLERS.get(msg_type)
    if handler:
        response = await handler(context) if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(handler) else handler(context)
        return response or {}
    return {}

---------------- FILE: app/services/slack_service.py ----------------
import httpx
from typing import Any, Optional
from app.core.config import NANGO_SECRET_KEY, NANGO_BASE_URL  # Changed

async def post_to_slack_via_nango(config: Any, text: str, thread_ts: Optional[str] = None) -> Optional[str]:
    """Sends a message to Slack using Nango's Proxy endpoint."""
    url = f"{NANGO_BASE_URL}/proxy/chat.postMessage"
    headers = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {NANGO_SECRET_KEY}",
        "Connection-Id": config.nango_connection_id,
        "Provider-Config-Key": config.nango_integration_id,
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
    }
    payload = {"channel": config.slack_channel_id, "text": text}
    if thread_ts:
        payload["thread_ts"] = thread_ts

    async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
        try:
            resp = await client.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload)
            print(f"Nango proxy status: {resp.status_code}")
            print(f"Nango proxy response: {resp.text[:300]}")
            data = resp.json()
            if data.get("ok"):
                return data.get("ts")
            print(f"❌ Nango/Slack Error: {data}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"❌ Nango Proxy request failed: {e}")
    return None
---------------- FILE: app/services/vapi_handlers.py ----------------
import asyncio
import json
import re
import os
from typing import Any, Optional
from groq import Groq

from app.core.state import call_sessions
from app.core.config import VAPI_BASE_ASSISTANT_ID
from app.core.business_registry import get_config_by_ani
from app.services.slack_service import post_to_slack_via_nango

groq_client = Groq(api_key=os.getenv("GROQ_API_KEY"))

def _pretty_json(data: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    return json.dumps(data, indent=2, ensure_ascii=True)

async def background_slack_init(config: Any, text: str, call_id: str):
    """Creates the parent Slack thread and stores the TS in the session."""
    ts = await post_to_slack_via_nango(config, text)
    if ts and call_id in call_sessions:
        call_sessions[call_id]["slack_thread_ts"] = ts
        print(f"✅ Parent Slack thread created: {ts}")

async def background_post_summary(session: dict, transcript_text: str):
    """Heavy lifting: LLM summarization and Slack posting in the background."""
    try:
        config = session.get("config")
        
        # Run the synchronous Groq call in a thread to prevent blocking the event loop
        def fetch_summary():
            return groq_client.chat.completions.create(
                model="llama-3.1-8b-instant",
                messages=[
                    {"role": "system", "content": "Summarize this call transcript professionally in 3-4 bullet points."},
                    {"role": "user", "content": f"Transcript:\n{transcript_text}"}
                ]
            )
            
        chat_completion = await asyncio.to_thread(fetch_summary)
        summary_text = chat_completion.choices[0].message.content

        await post_to_slack_via_nango(
            config=config,
            text=f"📋 *Final Call Summary:*\n{summary_text}",
            thread_ts=session.get("slack_thread_ts")
        )
        print(f"✅ Summary posted for thread {session.get('slack_thread_ts')}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Error in background summary: {e}")

def _append_transcript(call_id: str, role: str, text: str) -> None:
    if call_id in call_sessions and text:
        call_sessions[call_id]["transcript"].append({"role": role, "text": text})

def _handle_assistant_started(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    call_id = ctx["call_id"]
    call = ctx["call"]
    control_url = call.get("monitor", {}).get("controlUrl")
    
    if call_id in call_sessions:
        call_sessions[call_id]["control_url"] = control_url
    
    print(f"Session started for {call_id} | control_url: {control_url}")
    return None

def _handle_conversation_update(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    return None

async def _handle_assistant_request(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    call = ctx["call"]
    call_id = ctx["call_id"]
    customer_number = ctx["customer_number"]
    
    # GUARD: Prevent double initialization if VAPI retries the request
    if call_id in call_sessions and call_sessions[call_id].get("slack_thread_ts"):
        return None

    # Extract Owner Number (ANI) from SIP Diversion
    sip_headers = call.get("phoneCallProviderDetails", {}).get("sip", {}).get("headers", {})
    diversion = sip_headers.get("Diversion", "") or call.get("sipHeaders", {}).get("Diversion", "")
    
    match = re.search(r"sip:(\+?\d+)", diversion)
    owner_number = match.group(1) if match else "9611896916" # Fallback for testing

    # Lookup Business via Registry
    config, matched = get_config_by_ani(owner_number)
    print(f"📞 Call for: {config.display_name} (Connection: {config.nango_connection_id})")

    # Initialize session state
    call_sessions[call_id] = {
        "customer_number": customer_number,
        "slack_thread_ts": None,
        "config": config,
        "transcript": []
    }

    # Trigger Slack Alert in Background
    if config.nango_connection_id and config.slack_channel_id:
        msg = f"📞 *Incoming Call*\n*Business:* {config.display_name}\n*Customer:* {customer_number}"
        asyncio.create_task(background_slack_init(config, msg, call_id))

    # Return Assistant Config to Vapi
    if VAPI_BASE_ASSISTANT_ID:
        return {
            "assistantId": VAPI_BASE_ASSISTANT_ID,
            "assistantOverrides": {
                "variableValues": {
                    **config.system_prompt_var,
                    "callerNumber": customer_number
                },
                "firstMessage": config.first_message,
            }
        }
    
    return {
        "assistant": {
            "name": config.display_name,
            "firstMessage": config.first_message,
            "model": {
                "provider": "openai",
                "model": "gpt-4o-mini",
                "messages": [{"role": "system", "content": f"Assistant for {config.display_name}"}]
            }
        }
    }

def _handle_status_update(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    print(f"Call status: {ctx['message'].get('status', '')}")
    return None

def _handle_tool_calls(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    message = ctx["message"]
    tool_calls = message.get("toolCallList", [])
    if not tool_calls:
        tool_calls = [
            entry.get("toolCall", {}) for entry in message.get("toolWithToolCallList", []) if entry.get("toolCall")
        ]

    results = []
    for tool_call in tool_calls:
        tool_name = tool_call.get("name", "")
        results.append({
            "name": tool_name,
            "toolCallId": tool_call.get("id", ""),
            "result": json.dumps({"status": "ok", "message": f"Tool {tool_name} executed"}),
        })
    return {"results": results}

async def _handle_end_of_call_report(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    call_id = ctx["call_id"]
    
    # pop to clean up memory immediately
    session = call_sessions.pop(call_id, {})  
    
    transcript = session.get("transcript", [])
    config = session.get("config")
    
    if not transcript or not config or not config.slack_channel_id:
        print(f"Call {call_id} ended — no transcript or Slack config")
        return None
    
    # Format transcript for LLM
    transcript_text = "\n".join([f"{entry['role'].capitalize()}: {entry['text']}" for entry in transcript])
    
    # Run the summary in the background so we can return 200 to VAPI instantly
    asyncio.create_task(background_post_summary(session, transcript_text))

    return {"status": "processing_summary"}

def _handle_hang(_: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    print("Assistant failed to respond in time/hung up.")
    return None

def _handle_speech_update(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    return None

async def _handle_transcript(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    message = ctx["message"]
    call_id = ctx["call_id"]
    role = message.get("role", "assistant")
    
    # VAPI sometimes sends transcript text in different fields based on the event
    text = message.get("transcript") or message.get("text") or ""
    
    # Send only final transcript segments to Slack thread AND save to memory
    if message.get("transcriptType") == "final" and call_id in call_sessions:
        session = call_sessions[call_id]
        
        if text:
            # FIX: This is now safely inside the "final" check!
            _append_transcript(call_id, role, text)
            
            if session.get("slack_thread_ts"):
                icon = "🤖" if role == "assistant" else "👤"
                asyncio.create_task(post_to_slack_via_nango(
                    config=session["config"],
                    text=f"{icon} *{role.capitalize()}:* {text}",
                    thread_ts=session["slack_thread_ts"]
                ))
            
    return None

# Event handlers dictionary
EVENT_HANDLERS: dict[str, Any] = {
    "assistant.started": _handle_assistant_started,
    "conversation-update": _handle_conversation_update,
    "assistant-request": _handle_assistant_request,
    "status-update": _handle_status_update,
    "tool-calls": _handle_tool_calls,
    "end-of-call-report": _handle_end_of_call_report,
    "hang": _handle_hang,
    "speech-update": _handle_speech_update,
    "transcript": _handle_transcript,
    'transcript[transcriptType="final"]': _handle_transcript,
}

---------------- FILE: SETUP_INSTRUCTIONS.md ----------------
# SuperOwl Inbound POC 

This prototype allows you to test:
1. Live Call Transcript streaming to Slack.
2. Owner Whisper (type in Slack → AI hears it).
3. Owner Takeover (type "takeover" → Call transfers to your phone).

## Prerequisites
- WSL (Ubuntu) installed on Windows.
- A free **VAPI.ai** account with credits.
- A **Slack Workspace** where you are an admin.
- **ngrok** installed (`sudo apt install ngrok`).

---

## Phase 1: Slack Setup (Do this first)

1. **Create a Slack App**:
   - Go to [api.slack.com/apps](https://api.slack.com/apps) → **Create New App** → **From scratch**.
   - App Name: `SuperOwl-Test`
   - Workspace: Select your test workspace.

2. **Add Permissions**:
   - Go to **OAuth & Permissions** → **Bot Token Scopes**.
   - Add these scopes: `chat:write`, `chat:write.public`, `app_mentions:read`.
   - Scroll up and click **Reinstall App** to authorize.
   - Copy the **Bot User OAuth Token** (starts with `xoxb-...`). Save this for later.

3. **Enable Events API**:
   - Go to **Event Subscriptions**.
   - Toggle **Enable Events** to ON.
   - **Request URL**: Leave blank for now (we will fill this after starting the server).
   - Under **Subscribe to bot events**, add: `message.channels`.
   - Click **Save Changes**.

4. **Create Channels**:
   - In your Slack, create two channels: `#calls-live` and `#calls-transcripts`.
   - Invite your bot to both: Type `/invite @SuperOwl-Test` in both channels.
   - Right-click `#calls-transcripts` → **View channel details** → Copy the **Channel ID** (starts with `C`).

---

## Phase 2: VAPI Setup

1. **Get Credentials**:
   - Log in to [VAPI.ai](https://vapi.ai).
   - Copy your **API Key**.
   - Create a new **Assistant** (or use an existing one). Ensure its System Prompt uses variables like `{{businessName}}`.
   - Copy the **Assistant ID**.
   - Go to **Phone Numbers** → Buy/Add a number. Copy the **Phone Number ID**.
   - **Important**: Set the Phone Number's **Server URL** to your ngrok URL + `/vapi/server` (e.g., `https://xxxx.ngrok-free.app/vapi/server`). *You will get this URL in Phase 3.*

---

## Phase 3: Run the Project

1. **Install Dependencies**:
   ```bash
   cd superowl_inbound
   uv sync
   ```


Then in  .env,paste this accordingly:
# VAPI
VAPI_API_KEY=YOUR_VAPI_KEY_HERE
VAPI_BASE_ASSISTANT_ID=YOUR_ASSISTANT_ID_HERE
VAPI_PHONE_NUMBER_ID=YOUR_PHONE_NUMBER_ID_HERE

# Nango (Optional if using direct Slack token below)
NANGO_SECRET_KEY=
NANGO_BASE_URL=https://api.nango.dev

# Slack
SLACK_BOT_TOKEN=xoxb-YOUR_TOKEN_FROM_PHASE_1
SLACK_CHANNEL_ID=C-YOUR_CHANNEL_ID_FROM_PHASE_1

# Business Config
OWNER_PHONE=+91YOUR_MOBILE_NUMBER




 # start the server
 ```bash
 uv run uvicorn main:app --reload --port 8001
 ```

 # open a new terminal
```bash
ngrok http 8001
```

from pydantic import BaseModel

class BusinessConfig(BaseModel):
    display_name: str 
    first_message: str 
    system_prompt_var: dict[str, str]
    nango_connection_id: str | None = None
    nango_integration_id: str = "slack"
    slack_channel_id: str | None = None
    fallback_number: str | None = None  # <-- Added this back!

FALLBACK_CONFIG = BusinessConfig(
    display_name="SuperOwl Assistant",
    first_message="Hello! How can I help you today?",
    system_prompt_var={"businessName": "SuperOwl"},
    fallback_number=None
)

def get_config_by_ani(ani: str | None) -> tuple[BusinessConfig, bool]:
    normalized = "".join(filter(str.isdigit, ani or ""))[-10:]
    biz_data = get_business(normalized)
    
    if biz_data:
        return BusinessConfig(
            display_name=biz_data["display_name"],
            first_message=f"Hi! This is {biz_data['display_name']}. How can I help?",
            system_prompt_var={
                "businessName": biz_data["display_name"],
                "city": biz_data.get("city", "Bengaluru"),
                "hours": biz_data.get("hours", "regular business hours"),
                "services": biz_data.get("services", "our services")
            },
            nango_connection_id=biz_data.get("nango_connection_id"),
            slack_channel_id=biz_data.get("slack_channel_id"),
            fallback_number=biz_data.get("fallback_number", f"+91{normalized}")  # <-- Map it here so the takeover branch can read it
        ), True
    
    return FALLBACK_CONFIG, Falseimport os

# Configuration
NANGO_SECRET_KEY = os.getenv("NANGO_SECRET_KEY")

import os 

DB_FILE = "businesses.json"

def get_business(phone: str):
    if not os.path.exists(DB_FILE):
        return None
    
    try:
        with open(DB_FILE, "r") as f:
            content = f.read().strip()
            if not content:
                return None
            data = json.loads(content)
            return data.get(phone)
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        print(f"❌ Error reading {DB_FILE}, file may be corrupted")
        return None
    
def save_business(phone: str, connection_id: str, display_name: str, slack_channel_id: str):
    data = {}
    if os.path.exists(DB_FILE):
        try:
            with open(DB_FILE, "r") as f:
                content = f.read().strip()
                if content:
                    data = json.loads(content)
        except json.JSONDecodeError:
            print(f"⚠️ Corrupted {DB_FILE}, creating new one")
            data = {}
    
    data[phone] = {
        "display_name": display_name,
        "nango_connection_id": connection_id,
        "nango_integration_id": "slack",
        "slack_channel_id": slack_channel_id,
        "system_prompt": f"You are a helpful assistant for {display_name}."
    }
    
    with open(DB_FILE, "w") as f:
        json.dump(data, f, indent=4)

@router.get("/", response_class=HTMLResponse)
async def serve_index():

@router.get("/connect/session")
async def create_nango_session(phone: str):
    """Step 1: Frontend calls this to get a Nango session token"""
    connection_id = f"conn_{phone}"
    async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
        resp = await client.post(
            f"{NANGO_BASE_URL}/connect/sessions",
            headers={
                "Authorization": f"Bearer {NANGO_SECRET_KEY}",
                "Content-Type": "application/json"
            },
            json={
                "end_user": {"id": connection_id},
                "allowed_integrations": ["slack"],
            }
        )
        print(f"Nango session response: {resp.status_code} — {resp.text}")
        if resp.status_code != 200:
            return {"error": "Could not create session"}
        return resp.json()["data"]


@router.get("/slack/channels")
async def list_slack_channels(phone: str):
    """Step 2: After OAuth, frontend calls this to show channel dropdown"""
    # Fix: Nango proxy URL is /proxy/{method}, NOT /proxy/slack/{method}
    url = f"{NANGO_BASE_URL}/proxy/conversations.list"
    headers = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {NANGO_SECRET_KEY}",
        "Connection-Id": f"conn_{phone}",
        "Provider-Config-Key": "slack"
    }
    async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
        resp = await client.get(url, headers=headers)
        print(f"Slack channels response: {resp.status_code} — {resp.text[:200]}")
        data = resp.json()
        channels = data.get("channels", [])
        # Return only public, non-archived channels for the dropdown
        return [
            {"name": c["name"], "id": c["id"]}
            for c in channels
            if not c.get("is_archived", False)
        ]

    )

    return {"status": "ok"}
