from app.core.state import call_sessions
import asyncio, httpx

router = APIRouter()

@router.post("/slack/events")
async def slack_events(request: Request):
    body = await request.json()
    
    # 1. Handle Slack URL verification challenge
    if body.get("type") == "url_verification":
        challenge = body.get("challenge")
        print("Slack URL Verified!!")
        return {"challenge": challenge}
        
    event = body.get("event", {})
    
    # 2. Handle message events
    event_type = event.get("type")
    text = event.get("text", "")
    thread_ts = event.get("thread_ts")
    bot_id = event.get("bot_id")

    # RULE: Must be a message, must be in a thread, and MUST NOT be from our own bot
    if event_type == "message" and thread_ts and not bot_id:
        print(f"\n🗣️ OWNER MESSAGE RECEIVED: {text}")
        
        # 3. Find which call this thread_ts belongs to
        target_call_id = None
        target_control_url = None
        
        for call_id, session_data in call_sessions.items():
            if session_data.get("slack_thread_ts") == thread_ts:
                target_call_id = call_id
                target_control_url = session_data.get("control_url")
                break
                
        if target_call_id and target_control_url:
            print(f"✅ Matched to Call ID: {target_call_id}")
            print(f"🔗 Ready to inject via Control URL: {target_control_url}")
            
            clean_text = text.lower().strip()
            
            # --- TAKEOVER ---
            if clean_text == "takeover" or clean_text == "!takeover":
                fallback_number = call_sessions[target_call_id]["config"].fallback_number
                payload = {
                    "type": "transfer",
                    "destination": {
                        "type": "sip",
                        "sipUri": f"sip:{fallback_number}@40942180.sip.vobiz.ai"
                    }
                }
                print("🔀 TAKEOVER payload built")
            
            # --- END CALL ---
            elif clean_text in ["end", "reject", "stop", "hangup"]:
                payload = {
                    "type": "end-call",
                    "message": {
                        "role": "system",
                        "content": (
                            "The owner has asked to end this call. "
                            "Say: 'I'm sorry, the owner is not available right now. Please call back later. Goodbye!' "
                            "Then call end_call_tool immediately."
                        )
                    }
                }
                print("🗣️ WHISPER payload built")
            
            # --- WHISPER (default) ---
            else:
                payload = {
                    "type": "add-message",
                    "message": {
                        "role": "system",
                        "content": f"The business owner just whispered: '{text}'. Naturally incorporate this into your next response to the customer."
                    }
                }
                print("🗣️ WHISPER payload built")

            # Fire the command to VAPI (works for all three cases)
            async def send_command():
                async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
                    try:
                        resp = await client.post(target_control_url, json=payload)
                        print(f"🎯 Command injected! Vapi replied: {resp.status_code}")
                    except Exception as e:
                        print(f"❌ Failed to inject command: {e}")
                        
            asyncio.create_task(send_command())
            
        else:
            print("⚠️ Could not find an active call for this Slack thread.")

    # Always return 200 OK so Slack doesn't retry sending the message
    return {"status": "ok"}from fastapi import APIRouter, Request
from app.services.vapi_handlers import EVENT_HANDLERS  # Changed
import asyncio

router = APIRouter()

@router.post("/vapi/server")
async def vapi_server(request: Request):
    body = await request.json()
    message = body.get("message", {})
    msg_type = message.get("type", "")
    
    context = {
        "call_id": message.get("call", {}).get("id", "unknown"),
        "customer_number": message.get("call", {}).get("customer", {}).get("number", ""),
        "call": message.get("call", {}),
        "message": message
    }

    handler = EVENT_HANDLERS.get(msg_type)
    if handler:
        response = await handler(context) if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(handler) else handler(context)
        return response or {}
    return {}import httpx
from typing import Any, Optional
from app.core.config import NANGO_SECRET_KEY, NANGO_BASE_URL  # Changed

async def post_to_slack_via_nango(config: Any, text: str, thread_ts: Optional[str] = None) -> Optional[str]:
    """Sends a message to Slack using Nango's Proxy endpoint."""
    url = f"{NANGO_BASE_URL}/proxy/chat.postMessage"
    headers = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {NANGO_SECRET_KEY}",
        "Connection-Id": config.nango_connection_id,
        "Provider-Config-Key": config.nango_integration_id,
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
    }
    payload = {"channel": config.slack_channel_id, "text": text}
    if thread_ts:
        payload["thread_ts"] = thread_ts

    async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
        try:
            resp = await client.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload)
            print(f"Nango proxy status: {resp.status_code}")
            print(f"Nango proxy response: {resp.text[:300]}")
            data = resp.json()
            if data.get("ok"):
                return data.get("ts")
            print(f"❌ Nango/Slack Error: {data}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"❌ Nango Proxy request failed: {e}")
    return Noneimport asyncio
import json
import re
import os
from typing import Any, Optional
from groq import Groq

from app.core.state import call_sessions
from app.core.config import VAPI_BASE_ASSISTANT_ID
from app.core.business_registry import get_config_by_ani
from app.services.slack_service import post_to_slack_via_nango

groq_client = Groq(api_key=os.getenv("GROQ_API_KEY"))

def _pretty_json(data: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    return json.dumps(data, indent=2, ensure_ascii=True)

async def background_slack_init(config: Any, text: str, call_id: str):
    """Creates the parent Slack thread and stores the TS in the session."""
    ts = await post_to_slack_via_nango(config, text)
    if ts and call_id in call_sessions:
        call_sessions[call_id]["slack_thread_ts"] = ts
        print(f"✅ Parent Slack thread created: {ts}")

async def background_post_summary(session: dict, transcript_text: str):
    """Heavy lifting: LLM summarization and Slack posting in the background."""
    try:
        config = session.get("config")
        
        # Run the synchronous Groq call in a thread to prevent blocking the event loop
        def fetch_summary():
            return groq_client.chat.completions.create(
                model="llama-3.1-8b-instant",
                messages=[
                    {"role": "system", "content": "Summarize this call transcript professionally in 3-4 bullet points."},
                    {"role": "user", "content": f"Transcript:\n{transcript_text}"}
                ]
            )
            
        chat_completion = await asyncio.to_thread(fetch_summary)
        summary_text = chat_completion.choices[0].message.content

        await post_to_slack_via_nango(
            config=config,
            text=f"📋 *Final Call Summary:*\n{summary_text}",
            thread_ts=session.get("slack_thread_ts")
        )
        print(f"✅ Summary posted for thread {session.get('slack_thread_ts')}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Error in background summary: {e}")

def _append_transcript(call_id: str, role: str, text: str) -> None:
    if call_id in call_sessions and text:
        call_sessions[call_id]["transcript"].append({"role": role, "text": text})

def _handle_assistant_started(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    call_id = ctx["call_id"]
    call = ctx["call"]
    control_url = call.get("monitor", {}).get("controlUrl")
    
    if call_id in call_sessions:
        call_sessions[call_id]["control_url"] = control_url
    
    print(f"Session started for {call_id} | control_url: {control_url}")
    return None

def _handle_conversation_update(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    return None

async def _handle_assistant_request(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    call = ctx["call"]
    call_id = ctx["call_id"]
    customer_number = ctx["customer_number"]
    
    # GUARD: Prevent double initialization if VAPI retries the request
    if call_id in call_sessions and call_sessions[call_id].get("slack_thread_ts"):
        return None

    # Extract Owner Number (ANI) from SIP Diversion
    sip_headers = call.get("phoneCallProviderDetails", {}).get("sip", {}).get("headers", {})
    diversion = sip_headers.get("Diversion", "") or call.get("sipHeaders", {}).get("Diversion", "")
    
    match = re.search(r"sip:(\+?\d+)", diversion)
    owner_number = match.group(1) if match else "9611896916" # Fallback for testing

    # Lookup Business via Registry
    config, matched = get_config_by_ani(owner_number)
    print(f"📞 Call for: {config.display_name} (Connection: {config.nango_connection_id})")

    # Initialize session state
    call_sessions[call_id] = {
        "customer_number": customer_number,
        "slack_thread_ts": None,
        "config": config,
        "transcript": []
    }

    # Trigger Slack Alert in Background
    if config.nango_connection_id and config.slack_channel_id:
        msg = f"📞 *Incoming Call*\n*Business:* {config.display_name}\n*Customer:* {customer_number}"
        asyncio.create_task(background_slack_init(config, msg, call_id))

    # Return Assistant Config to Vapi
    if VAPI_BASE_ASSISTANT_ID:
        return {
            "assistantId": VAPI_BASE_ASSISTANT_ID,
            "assistantOverrides": {
                "variableValues": {
                    **config.system_prompt_var,
                    "callerNumber": customer_number
                },
                "firstMessage": config.first_message,
            }
        }
    
    return {
        "assistant": {
            "name": config.display_name,
            "firstMessage": config.first_message,
            "model": {
                "provider": "openai",
                "model": "gpt-4o-mini",
                "messages": [{"role": "system", "content": f"Assistant for {config.display_name}"}]
            }
        }
    }

def _handle_status_update(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    print(f"Call status: {ctx['message'].get('status', '')}")
    return None

def _handle_tool_calls(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    message = ctx["message"]
    tool_calls = message.get("toolCallList", [])
    if not tool_calls:
        tool_calls = [
            entry.get("toolCall", {}) for entry in message.get("toolWithToolCallList", []) if entry.get("toolCall")
        ]

    results = []
    for tool_call in tool_calls:
        tool_name = tool_call.get("name", "")
        results.append({
            "name": tool_name,
            "toolCallId": tool_call.get("id", ""),
            "result": json.dumps({"status": "ok", "message": f"Tool {tool_name} executed"}),
        })
    return {"results": results}

async def _handle_end_of_call_report(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    call_id = ctx["call_id"]
    
    # pop to clean up memory immediately
    session = call_sessions.pop(call_id, {})  
    
    transcript = session.get("transcript", [])
    config = session.get("config")
    
    if not transcript or not config or not config.slack_channel_id:
        print(f"Call {call_id} ended — no transcript or Slack config")
        return None
    
    # Format transcript for LLM
    transcript_text = "\n".join([f"{entry['role'].capitalize()}: {entry['text']}" for entry in transcript])
    
    # Run the summary in the background so we can return 200 to VAPI instantly
    asyncio.create_task(background_post_summary(session, transcript_text))

    return {"status": "processing_summary"}

def _handle_hang(_: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    print("Assistant failed to respond in time/hung up.")
    return None

def _handle_speech_update(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    return None

async def _handle_transcript(ctx: dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
    message = ctx["message"]
    call_id = ctx["call_id"]
    role = message.get("role", "assistant")
    
    # VAPI sometimes sends transcript text in different fields based on the event
    text = message.get("transcript") or message.get("text") or ""
    
    # Send only final transcript segments to Slack thread AND save to memory
    if message.get("transcriptType") == "final" and call_id in call_sessions:
        session = call_sessions[call_id]
        
        if text:
            # FIX: This is now safely inside the "final" check!
            _append_transcript(call_id, role, text)
            
            if session.get("slack_thread_ts"):
                icon = "🤖" if role == "assistant" else "👤"
                asyncio.create_task(post_to_slack_via_nango(
                    config=session["config"],
                    text=f"{icon} *{role.capitalize()}:* {text}",
                    thread_ts=session["slack_thread_ts"]
                ))
            
    return None

# Event handlers dictionary
EVENT_HANDLERS: dict[str, Any] = {
    "assistant.started": _handle_assistant_started,
    "conversation-update": _handle_conversation_update,
    "assistant-request": _handle_assistant_request,
    "status-update": _handle_status_update,
    "tool-calls": _handle_tool_calls,
    "end-of-call-report": _handle_end_of_call_report,
    "hang": _handle_hang,
    "speech-update": _handle_speech_update,
    "transcript": _handle_transcript,
    'transcript[transcriptType="final"]': _handle_transcript,
}from fastapi import FastAPI
from app.routers import slack_events, vapi_webhook, onboarding

app = FastAPI()

# Include routers
app.include_router(vapi_webhook.router)
app.include_router(onboarding.router)
app.include_router(slack_events.router)

}# SuperOwl Inbound POC 

This prototype allows you to test:
1. Live Call Transcript streaming to Slack.
2. Owner Whisper (type in Slack → AI hears it).
3. Owner Takeover (type "takeover" → Call transfers to your phone).

## Prerequisites
- WSL (Ubuntu) installed on Windows.
- A free **VAPI.ai** account with credits.
- A **Slack Workspace** where you are an admin.
- **ngrok** installed (`sudo apt install ngrok`).

---

## Phase 1: Slack Setup (Do this first)

1. **Create a Slack App**:
   - Go to [api.slack.com/apps](https://api.slack.com/apps) → **Create New App** → **From scratch**.
   - App Name: `SuperOwl-Test`
   - Workspace: Select your test workspace.

2. **Add Permissions**:
   - Go to **OAuth & Permissions** → **Bot Token Scopes**.
   - Add these scopes: `chat:write`, `chat:write.public`, `app_mentions:read`.
   - Scroll up and click **Reinstall App** to authorize.
   - Copy the **Bot User OAuth Token** (starts with `xoxb-...`). Save this for later.

3. **Enable Events API**:
   - Go to **Event Subscriptions**.
   - Toggle **Enable Events** to ON.
   - **Request URL**: Leave blank for now (we will fill this after starting the server).
   - Under **Subscribe to bot events**, add: `message.channels`.
   - Click **Save Changes**.

4. **Create Channels**:
   - In your Slack, create two channels: `#calls-live` and `#calls-transcripts`.
   - Invite your bot to both: Type `/invite @SuperOwl-Test` in both channels.
   - Right-click `#calls-transcripts` → **View channel details** → Copy the **Channel ID** (starts with `C`).

---

## Phase 2: VAPI Setup

1. **Get Credentials**:
   - Log in to [VAPI.ai](https://vapi.ai).
   - Copy your **API Key**.
   - Create a new **Assistant** (or use an existing one). Ensure its System Prompt uses variables like `{{businessName}}`.
   - Copy the **Assistant ID**.
   - Go to **Phone Numbers** → Buy/Add a number. Copy the **Phone Number ID**.
   - **Important**: Set the Phone Number's **Server URL** to your ngrok URL + `/vapi/server` (e.g., `https://xxxx.ngrok-free.app/vapi/server`). *You will get this URL in Phase 3.*

---

## Phase 3: Run the Project

1. **Install Dependencies**:
   ```bash
   cd superowl_inbound
   uv sync
   ```


Then in  .env,paste this accordingly:
# VAPI
VAPI_API_KEY=YOUR_VAPI_KEY_HERE
VAPI_BASE_ASSISTANT_ID=YOUR_ASSISTANT_ID_HERE
VAPI_PHONE_NUMBER_ID=YOUR_PHONE_NUMBER_ID_HERE

# Nango (Optional if using direct Slack token below)
NANGO_SECRET_KEY=
NANGO_BASE_URL=https://api.nango.dev

# Slack
SLACK_BOT_TOKEN=xoxb-YOUR_TOKEN_FROM_PHASE_1
SLACK_CHANNEL_ID=C-YOUR_CHANNEL_ID_FROM_PHASE_1

# Business Config
OWNER_PHONE=+91YOUR_MOBILE_NUMBER




 # start the server
 ```bash
 uv run uvicorn main:app --reload --port 8001
 ```

 # open a new terminal
```bash
ngrok http 8001

        document.getElementById('slackForm').addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
            e.preventDefault();

            const phone = document.getElementById('phone').value.trim();
            const name = document.getElementById('name').value.trim();
            const resultDiv = document.getElementById('result');
            const loadingDiv = document.getElementById('loading');
            const submitBtn = document.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');

            resultDiv.textContent = '';

            if (!phone || !name) {
                resultDiv.textContent = 'Please enter both phone number and business name.';
                return;
            }

            loadingDiv.style.display = 'block';
            submitBtn.disabled = true;

            try {
                const resp = await fetch(`/connect/session?phone=${encodeURIComponent(phone)}`);
                const data = await resp.json();

                const connectLink = data?.data?.connect_link || data?.connect_link;

                if (connectLink) {
                    window.location.href = connectLink;
                } else {
                    resultDiv.textContent = 'Error: Could not get connect link from backend.';
                    console.error('Unexpected response:', data);
                }
            } catch (err) {
                resultDiv.textContent = 'Error: ' + err.message;
            } finally {
                loadingDiv.style.display = 'none';
                submitBtn.disabled = false;
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

---------------- FILE: agent/chat_agent.py ----------------
from json import load
import os 
import time
from groq import Groq

from kb.embeddings import search_chunks 
from dotenv import load_dotenv 
load_dotenv()

client=Groq(api_key=os.getenv("GROQ_API_KEY"))
system_prompt="""You are a helpful AI assistant for Troy Blocks, an educational wooden toy company based in Bengaluru.
Answer questions based ONLY on the provided context from the knowledge base.
If the answer is not in the context, say "I don't have that information, please contact us at 9731737460."
Be professional, friendly, and concise.
Do not make up information.
If user is a preschool owner, emphasize structured curriculum and workshop model.
If user is a parent, highlight creativity, birthday parties, and learning through play.do not be presumptous,and dont exceed more than 3 lines.
If the conversation leans towards the purpose of knowing more,or booking,only then callback."""
    
def chat(question:str,hist:list[dict],namespace:str="superowl-proto")->str:
    chunks=search_chunks(query=question,namespace=namespace,top_k=3)
    context="\n\n".join(
    [f"[Source :{c['page_title']}]\n{c['text']}"
    for c  in chunks]
    )
    messages=[
        {
            "role":"system",
            "content":system_prompt
        },
        *hist,
       {
            "role": "user",
            "content": f"""Context from knowledge base:{context} Customer question: {question}"""
        }
    ]
    response=client.chat.completions.create(messages=messages,model="llama-3.1-8b-instant",temperature=0.2)
    return response.choices[0].message.content

app = FastAPI()


def build_transfer_sip_uri() -> str | None:
    """
    Build transfer SIP URI from environment variables.

    Priority:
    1. TRANSFER_SIP_URI (full URI, recommended)
    2. OWNER_PHONE + TRANSFER_SIP_DOMAIN
    """
    explicit_uri = os.getenv("TRANSFER_SIP_URI")
    if explicit_uri:
        return explicit_uri

    owner_phone = os.getenv("OWNER_PHONE")
    sip_domain = os.getenv("TRANSFER_SIP_DOMAIN")

    if owner_phone and sip_domain:
        return f"sip:{owner_phone}@{sip_domain}"

    return None

# Function Call Rules

You have access to the following tools.

### search_knowledge_base

Use this tool **if the customer asks something not covered in the business knowledge above**.

Example:

* product details
* special requests
* unusual event types

**If KB search returns no results:**

Say: "Let me get our team's direct contact for that question — would a callback be helpful?"

**If KB search fails or times out:**

Say: "I don't have that detail on hand, but I'll make sure the team can help when we talk. Is there anything else?"

Call:

search_knowledge_base(query)

---

### notify_owner

Call this tool when the customer:

• clearly wants to book
• asks to speak to the owner
• shows strong interest
• asks about immediate availability
• mentions urgency
• asks to confirm booking

When calling notify_owner, pass:

* customer_name
* call_summary
* reason_for_flagging

Example summary:

"Parent wants birthday party activity for around fifteen kids next Saturday evening at Whitefield."

After calling notify_owner say:

"Let me check availability with our team. Please hold for just a moment."

Then remain silent until instruction arrives.

---

### transfer_call_tool

If the system confirms the owner is available:

Say:

"Great news! The owner is available and ready to speak with you. Connecting you now, please hold."

Then call:

transfer_call_tool()

---

### end_call_tool

If the owner is unavailable:

Say:

"Our team is a little occupied at the moment but they will call you back shortly. Thank you so much for your interest in Troy Blocks!"

Then call:

end_call_tool()

---

# Voice Behavior Rules

## Speech Normalization

Speak numbers naturally.

Examples:

399 → three hundred ninety nine
499 → four hundred ninety nine
3990 → three thousand nine hundred ninety

Do not say:

* "Rs"
* "rupees"
* digits individually

---

# Phone Number Rules

Phone numbers must be spoken **digit by digit**.

Example:

"nine eight seven, six five four, three two one zero"

Never add country code.

---

# Turn Discipline

• Ask **one question at a time**
• **Wait 2 seconds for response**
• If no response after 2 seconds: **repeat the question once, softly** (e.g., "Sorry, did you have a chance to think about that?")
• If **still no response** after second ask: **assume "no" or offer callback** ("No worries, we can call you back!")
• If caller says "one moment", **wait silently for 5 seconds**, then gently: "Still here whenever you're ready."
• Never ask same question 3+ times in a row

---

# Identity Rule

If asked who you are:

"I'm a virtual assistant helping coordinate Troy activity bookings."

If asked if you are AI:

"Yes, I'm a virtual assistant helping with booking coordination."

Keep explanations short.

---

# Silence Handling

**If customer goes silent > 3 seconds:**

Say: "I'm still here. Are you there?" or "Hello?"

**If silence continues > 2 more seconds:**

Say: "It seems like we lost the connection. No worries — we'll call you back!"

Then call end_call_tool().

---

# Closing

When ending the conversation:

"Thank you for your interest in Troy activities. Have a wonderful day.""",
    }
}

ACTIVE_TENANT_ID = "exnnpDvj3CUqdKdZb6SBNQM9gld2"


def get_tenant():
    return TENANT_CONFIG[ACTIVE_TENANT_ID]


# ─── VAPI HELPERS ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

async def make_vapi_call(
    assistant_id: str,
    phone: str,
    name: str,
    system_prompt: str,
    first_message: str,
    transfer_number: str | None = None
):
    """
    Fire an outbound VAPI call.
    Injects system_prompt + first_message via assistantOverrides.
    Optionally injects transfer destination for transfer_call_tool.
    """
    url = "https://api.vapi.ai/call"
    headers = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.getenv('VAPI_API_KEY')}",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    }

    assistant_overrides = {
        "firstMessage": first_message,
        "model": {
            "provider":"openai",
             "model": "gpt-4o-mini",
            "messages": [
                {
                    "role": "system",
                    "content": system_prompt
                }
            ]
        }
    }

    # Inject transfer destination if provided
    if transfer_number:
       assistant_overrides["tools:append"] = [
        {
            "type": "transferCall",
            "function":{
                "name":"transfer_call_tool",
                "description":"Transfer the customer call to the business owner. Only call this when explicitly instructed after owner confirms availability."
            },
            "destinations": [
                {
                    "type": "sip",
                    "sipUri": transfer_number,
                    "description": "Transfer to business owner"
                }
            ]
        }
    ]

    payload = {
        "assistantId": assistant_id,
        "phoneNumberId": os.getenv("VAPI_PHONE_NUMBER_ID"),
        "customer": {
            "number": phone,
            "name": name
        },
        "assistantOverrides": assistant_overrides
    }

    async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:
        resp = await client.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload)
    result = resp.json()
    print(f"VAPI call response ({resp.status_code}): {result}")
    return result

'''
async def send_background_message(customer_call_id: str, message: str):
    """
    Injects a system message into Ananya's active call mid-conversation.
    Used to tell Ananya to transfer or wrap up after owner decision.
    """
    session = call_sessions.get(customer_call_id, {})
    url = session.get("control_url")

'''
async def send_background_message(customer_call_id: str, message: str):
    """
    Injects a system message into Ananya's active call mid-conversation.
    Used to tell Ananya to transfer or wrap up after owner decision.
    """
    session = call_sessions.get(customer_call_id, {})
    url = session.get("control_url")

    if not url:
        print(f"No control URL found for call {customer_call_id}")
        return # Correctly placed inside the if-block

    headers = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.getenv('VAPI_API_KEY')}",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    }
    payload = {
        "type": "add-message",
        "message": {
            "role": "system",
            "content": message
        }
    }

    async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:
        # VAPI Control API uses POST to the monitor.controlUrl
        resp = await client.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload)

    print(f"Background message response: {resp.status_code} {resp.text}")
    return resp


async def command_customer_call(customer_call_id: str, decision: str):
    tenant = get_tenant()

    if decision == "yes":
        session = call_sessions.get(customer_call_id, {})
        control_url = session.get("control_url")

        if control_url:
            # Tell Ananya to say the handoff line
            await send_background_message(
                customer_call_id,
                "The owner is available. Say exactly: 'Great news! The owner is ready to speak with you. Connecting you now, please hold.' then stop speaking."
            )

            # Small delay to let Ananya finish speaking
            import asyncio
            await asyncio.sleep(4)

            # Execute the transfer directly from backend via controlUrl
            headers = {
                "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.getenv('VAPI_API_KEY')}",
                "Content-Type": "application/json"
            }
            transfer_payload = {
                "type": "transfer",
                "destination": {
                    "type": "sip",
                    "sipUri": tenant["transfer_sip_uri"]
                }
            }
            async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:
                resp = await client.post(control_url, headers=headers, json=transfer_payload)
            print(f"Transfer via controlUrl: {resp.status_code} {resp.text}")

        else:
            print(f"No control URL for call {customer_call_id}, cannot transfer")

    elif decision == "no":
        await send_background_message(
            customer_call_id,
            f"The owner is currently unavailable. "
            f"Say 'I'm sorry, our team at {tenant['business_name']} is a little occupied "
            f"at the moment. They will call you back shortly. Thank you so much!' then call end_call_tool."
        )

    elif decision == "voicemail":
        await send_background_message(
            customer_call_id,
            f"The owner did not pick up. "
            f"Say 'Our team seems to be unavailable right now but will call you back soon. "
            f"Thank you for your interest in {tenant['business_name']}!' then call end_call_tool."
        )




# ─── ROUTES ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

class CallbackRequest(BaseModel):
    name: str
    phone: str
    conversation_summary: str


@app.post("/trigger-call")
async def trigger_call(req: CallbackRequest):
    """
    Called by Streamlit frontend when customer requests callback.
    Fires Ananya call with full prompt + transfer destination injected.
    """
    tenant = get_tenant()

    if not tenant.get("transfer_sip_uri"):
        raise ValueError(
            "Transfer SIP destination is not configured. Set TRANSFER_SIP_URI or both OWNER_PHONE and TRANSFER_SIP_DOMAIN in .env"
        )

    # Full system prompt = base voice prompt + chat summary appended
    full_system_prompt = (
        tenant["voice_system_prompt"]
        + f"\n\n---\nChat Context (prior conversation with customer):\n{req.conversation_summary}"
    )

    # First message with customer name substituted
    first_message = tenant["voice_welcome_message"].replace(
        "{customer_name}", req.name
    )

    assistant_id = os.getenv("VAPI_ASSISTANT_ID")
    if not assistant_id:
        raise ValueError("VAPI_ASSISTANT_ID environment variable is not set")

    result = await make_vapi_call(
        assistant_id=assistant_id,
        phone=req.phone,
        name=req.name,
        system_prompt=full_system_prompt,
        first_message=first_message,
        transfer_number=tenant["transfer_sip_uri"],
    )

    call_id = result.get("id")
    if call_id:
        call_sessions[call_id] = {
            "customer_name": req.name,
            "customer_phone": req.phone,
            "conversation_summary": req.conversation_summary,
            "owner_call_triggered": False,
            "owner_call_id": None,
            "control_url": result.get("monitor", {}).get("controlUrl"),
        }
        print(f"Customer call triggered: {call_id}")

    return {"status": "call initiated", "call_id": call_id}


@app.post("/notify-owner")
async def notify_owner(request: Request):
    """
    Called by Ananya's notify_owner tool when she detects a high lead.
    Receives: customer_name, call_summary, lead_reason
    Fires Owner PA call with full context injected.
    """
    data = await request.json()
    print(f"notify_owner called: {data}")

    tool_call_id = data.get("message", {}).get("toolCallList", [{}])[0].get("id")
    arguments = data.get("message", {}).get("toolCallList", [{}])[0].get("function", {}).get("arguments", {})
    customer_name = arguments.get("customer_name", "the customer")
    call_summary = arguments.get("call_summary", "")
    lead_reason = arguments.get("lead_reason", "")
    customer_call_id = data.get("message", {}).get("call", {}).get("id")

    print(f"Customer: {customer_name}")
    print(f"Summary: {call_summary}")
    print(f"Reason: {lead_reason}")

    tenant = get_tenant()

    # Build Owner PA prompt with full customer context injected
    pa_system_prompt = f"""[Identity]
You are a professional, efficient AI assistant representing SuperOwl.
Your role is to inform the {tenant['business_name']} owner about a qualified lead
and get their availability decision quickly.

[Style]
- Concise, clear, and professional.
- No small talk. Stay focused.
- Sound human — use brief natural pauses.


[Customer Context]
Customer Name: {customer_name}
What they want: {call_summary}
Quality indicator: {lead_reason}

[Task]
1. Say: "Hello {tenant['owner_name']}, this is SuperOwl calling to inform of a lead. I have a qualified customer on the line."
2. Brief the owner: "{customer_name} wants to {call_summary}."
3. Ask: "Are you available to speak with them right now?"
4. Wait for response.
5. If YES: Say "Perfect, connecting you now." → call report_decision with decision="yes" → end call.
6. If NO: Say "No problem, I will let them know. Thank you!" → call report_decision with decision="no" → end call.
7. If no clear answer: ask once more. If still unclear → assume "no" → call report_decision with decision="no" → end call.

[Critical Rule]
Always call report_decision before ending.
Decision must be "yes" or "no" only. Nothing else."""

    pa_first_message = (
        f"Hello {tenant['owner_name']}, am I speaking to the owner of {tenant['business_name']}?"
    )

    owner_assistant_id = os.getenv("VAPI_OWNER_ASSISTANT_ID")
    if not owner_assistant_id:
        raise ValueError("VAPI_OWNER_ASSISTANT_ID environment variable is not set")

    # Fire Owner PA call
    owner_result = await make_vapi_call(
        assistant_id=owner_assistant_id,
        phone=tenant["owner_phone"],
        name=tenant["owner_name"],
        system_prompt=pa_system_prompt,
        first_message=pa_first_message,
    )

    owner_call_id = owner_result.get("id")
    if owner_call_id and customer_call_id:
        owner_to_customer[owner_call_id] = customer_call_id
        if customer_call_id in call_sessions:
            call_sessions[customer_call_id]["owner_call_triggered"] = True
            call_sessions[customer_call_id]["owner_call_id"] = owner_call_id
        print(f"Owner PA call triggered: {owner_call_id} → customer: {customer_call_id}")

    return {
        "results": [
            {
                "toolCallId": tool_call_id,
                "result": "Owner has been notified. Please hold while we check availability."
            }
        ]
    }


@app.post("/owner-decision")
async def owner_decision(request: Request):
    """
    Called by Owner PA's report_decision tool.
    Receives owner's yes/no/voicemail decision.
    Commands Ananya via background message injection.
    """
    data = await request.json()
    print(f"Owner decision received: {data}")

    tool_call_id = data.get("message", {}).get("toolCallList", [{}])[0].get("id")
    arguments = data.get("message", {}).get("toolCallList", [{}])[0].get("function", {}).get("arguments", {})
    decision = arguments.get("decision", "").lower()
    owner_call_id = data.get("message", {}).get("call", {}).get("id")

    print(f"Decision: {decision}, owner_call_id: {owner_call_id}")

    customer_call_id = owner_to_customer.get(owner_call_id)

    if customer_call_id:
        print(f"Commanding customer call: {customer_call_id} with decision: {decision}")
        await command_customer_call(customer_call_id, decision)
    else:
        print(f"No customer call found for owner call: {owner_call_id}")

    messages = {
        "yes": "Transfer initiated. Customer is being connected to the owner now.",
        "no": "Noted. Customer has been informed the team will call back shortly.",
    }

    return {
        "results": [
            {
                "toolCallId": tool_call_id,
                "result": messages.get(decision, "Decision recorded.")
            }
        ]
    }


@app.post("/vapi-webhook")
async def vapi_webhook(request: Request):
    """
    Receives all VAPI call events.
    Used for logging and call state tracking only.
    Qualification detection removed — Ananya decides via notify_owner tool.
    """
    data = await request.json()
    event_type = data.get("message", {}).get("type")
    call_id = data.get("message", {}).get("call", {}).get("id")

    print(f"VAPI webhook: {event_type} | call_id: {call_id}")

    if event_type == "call-ended":
        if call_id in call_sessions:
            print(f"Call ended. Session: {call_sessions[call_id]}")
        elif call_id in owner_to_customer.values():
            print(f"Owner PA call ended.")
    #this is for the summary
    if event_type == "end-of-call-report":
        msg = data.get("message", {})
        customer_name = msg.get("call", {}).get("customer", {}).get("name", "Unknown")
        customer_phone = msg.get("call", {}).get("customer", {}).get("number", "Unknown")
        duration_s = int(msg.get("durationSeconds", 0))
        duration_str = f"{duration_s // 60}m {duration_s % 60}s"
        ended_reason = msg.get("endedReason", "unknown")
        transcript = msg.get("transcript", "No transcript available.")
        started_at = msg.get("startedAt", "")[:16].replace("T", " ")
        assistant_name = msg.get("assistant", {}).get("name", "")

        print(f"END OF CALL REPORT: {assistant_name} | {customer_name} | {duration_str} | {ended_reason}")
        if assistant_name == "ananya":
            slack_url = os.getenv("SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL")
            if slack_url:
                slack_msg = {
                    "text": (
                        f"🤖 Ananya Call Report\n"
                        f"Customer: {customer_name} ({customer_phone})\n"
                        f"Duration: {duration_str}\n"
                        f"Reason: {ended_reason}\n"
                        f"Time: {started_at}\n\n"
                        f"Transcript:\n```\n{transcript}\n```"
                    )
                }
                def send_slack():
                    import httpx
                    r = httpx.post(slack_url, json=slack_msg, timeout=15.0,verify=False)
                    return r.status_code, r.text

                try:
                    loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
                    status, text = await loop.run_in_executor(None, send_slack)
                    print(f"Slack response: {status} {text}")
                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"Slack notification failed (non-fatal): {type(e).__name__}: {repr(e)}")
    return {"status": "ok"}


@app.post("/query-kb")
async def query_kb(request: Request):
    """
    Called by Ananya's search_knowledge_base tool during voice calls.
    Searches Pinecone and returns relevant KB chunks.
    """
    data = await request.json()

    tool_call_id = data.get("message", {}).get("toolCallList", [{}])[0].get("id", "")
    arguments = data.get("message", {}).get("toolCallList", [{}])[0].get("function", {}).get("arguments", {})
    query = arguments.get("query", "")

    if not query:
        query = data.get("query", "")

    print(f"KB query: {query}")

    tenant = get_tenant()

    from kb.embeddings import search_chunks
    chunks = search_chunks(query=query, namespace=tenant["kb_namespace"], top_k=3)
    context = "\n".join([c["text"] for c in chunks])

    print(f"KB result preview: {context[:200]}")

    if tool_call_id:
        return {
            "results": [
                {
                    "toolCallId": tool_call_id,
                    "result": context
                }
            ]
        }

    return {"result": context}

---------------- FILE: frontend/app.py ----------------
import streamlit as st
import sys
import os

sys.path.append(os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))))

from agent.chat_agent import chat

st.set_page_config(
    page_title="Troy Blocks Assistant",
    page_icon="🪵",
    layout="centered"
)

st.title("🪵 Troy Blocks AI Assistant")
st.caption("Ask me anything about Troy Blocks — products, pricing, activities, and more.")

if "history" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.history = []

if "messages" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.messages = []

if "show_callback" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.show_callback = False

# display all previous messages
for msg in st.session_state.messages:
    with st.chat_message(msg["role"]):
        st.write(msg["content"])


# show callback prompt when AI response suggests booking interest
if st.session_state.messages:
    last_ai_message = ""
    for msg in reversed(st.session_state.messages):
        if msg["role"] == "assistant":
            last_ai_message = msg["content"].lower()
            break

    callback_triggers = [
        "book", "booking", "callback", "call you", "speak with",
        "contact", "team", "schedule", "arrange", "connect"
    ]

    if any(trigger in last_ai_message for trigger in callback_triggers):
        with st.chat_message("assistant"):
            st.write("Would you like me to arrange a callback from our team? 📞")
            if st.button("Request a Callback"):
                st.session_state.show_callback = True

# callback form
if st.session_state.show_callback:
    with st.form("callback_form"):
        st.subheader("📞 Request a Callback")
        name = st.text_input("Your Name")
        phone = st.text_input("Phone Number")
        if not '+91' in phone:
            phone='+91'+phone
        submitted = st.form_submit_button("Submit")

    if submitted:
      if name and phone:
        import httpx

        # send to FastAPI backend which triggers VAPI call
        try:
            summary = "\n".join([
    f"{'Customer' if m['role'] == 'user' else 'Assistant'}: {m['content']}"
    for m in st.session_state.messages[-4:]
])
            resp = httpx.post(
                "http://localhost:8000/trigger-call",
                json={
                    "name": name,
                    "phone": phone,  # must be in format +91XXXXXXXXXX
                    "conversation_summary": str(st.session_state.messages[-4:])
                }
            )
            print("Backend response:", resp.json())
            st.success(f"Thanks {name}! We'll call you at {phone} shortly.")
            st.session_state.show_callback = False
        except Exception as e:
            st.error(f"Something went wrong: {e}")
      else:
        st.error("Please fill in both fields.")
# chat input — at bottom
question = st.chat_input("Ask a question...")

if question:
    with st.chat_message("user"):
        st.write(question)

    st.session_state.messages.append({"role": "user", "content": question})

    with st.spinner("Thinking..."):
        answer = chat(
            question=question,
            hist=st.session_state.history
        )

    with st.chat_message("assistant"):
        st.write(answer)

    st.session_state.messages.append({"role": "assistant", "content": answer})

    st.session_state.history.append({"role": "user", "content": question})
    st.session_state.history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": answer})

---------------- FILE: kb/embeddings.py ----------------
import os 
from pinecone import Pinecone
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()
pc=Pinecone(api_key=os.getenv("PINECONE_API_KEY"))
index = pc.Index(os.getenv("PINECONE_INDEX_NAME"))

def store_chunks(chunks:list[dict],namespace:str='troy_shop'):
    records=[]
    for chunk in chunks:
        records.append(
            {
                "id":chunk["id"],
                "text":chunk["text"],
                **chunk["metadata"]
            }
        )
    index.upsert_records(namespace=namespace, records=records)
    print(f"Stored {len(records)} chunks in namespace: {namespace}")

def search_chunks(query: str, namespace: str = "troy", top_k: int = 3):
    """
    query = customer's question
    top_k = how many matching chunks to return
    Returns list of matching text chunks
    """

    # search_records sends query text to Pinecone
    # Pinecone embeds query using same model
    # Returns top_k closest records
    results = index.search_records(
        namespace=namespace,
        query={"inputs": {"text": query}, "top_k": top_k},
        fields=["text", "page_title"]  # which metadata fields to return
    )

    # extract just the text from results
    chunks = []
    for match in results["result"]["hits"]:
        chunks.append({
            "text": match["fields"].get("text", ""),
            "page_title": match["fields"].get("page_title", "")
        })

    return chunks

    
---------------- FILE: kb/nango.py ----------------
import os
import httpx
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()

def get_nango_headers() -> dict:
    """
    Returns headers needed for Nango proxy calls.
    Nango uses these to inject the correct OAuth token automatically.
    No need to fetch token manually — Nango handles it.
    """
    return {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.getenv('NANGO_SECRET_KEY')}",
        "Connection-Id": os.getenv("NOTION_CONNECTION_ID"),
        "Provider-Config-Key": os.getenv("NOTION_INTEGRATION_ID"),
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    }

def get_nango_proxy_url(endpoint: str) -> str:
    """
    Builds Nango proxy URL for any Notion API endpoint.
    e.g. endpoint = "/v1/pages/abc123"
    returns "https://api.nango.dev/proxy/v1/pages/abc123"
    """
    return f"{os.getenv('NANGO_BASE_URL')}/proxy{endpoint}"
---------------- FILE: kb/notion_sync.py ----------------
import os
import asyncio
from notion_client import Client
from langchain_classic.text_splitter import RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter
from kb.embeddings import store_chunks
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()

# use token directly from .env
notion = Client(auth=os.getenv("NOTION_TOKEN"))

splitter = RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter(
    chunk_size=500,
    chunk_overlap=50
)

def extract_text_from_blocks(blocks: list) -> str:
    text = ""
    for block in blocks:
        block_type = block["type"]
        supported_types = [
            "paragraph",
            "heading_1", "heading_2", "heading_3",
            "bulleted_list_item", "numbered_list_item"
        ]
        if block_type in supported_types:
            rich_text = block[block_type]["rich_text"]
            for text_obj in rich_text:
                text += text_obj["plain_text"] + " "
        text += "\n"
    return text.strip()


def fetch_page_text(page_id: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
    page = notion.pages.retrieve(page_id=page_id)

    title = ""
    props = page["properties"]
    for prop in props.values():
        if prop["type"] == "title":
            for text_obj in prop["title"]:
                title += text_obj["plain_text"]
            break

    blocks_response = notion.blocks.children.list(block_id=page_id)
    blocks = blocks_response["results"]
    text = extract_text_from_blocks(blocks)
    return title, text


def sync_page_to_pinecone(page_id: str, namespace: str = "superowl-proto"):
    print(f"Fetching page {page_id} from Notion...")
    title, text = fetch_page_text(page_id)

    if not text.strip():
        print(f"Page {page_id} is empty, skipping.")
        return

    print(f"Page title: {title}")
    print(f"Text length: {len(text)} chars")

    text_chunks = splitter.split_text(text)
    print(f"Split into {len(text_chunks)} chunks")

    chunks = []
    for i, chunk_text in enumerate(text_chunks):
        chunks.append({
            "id": f"{page_id}_chunk_{i}",
            "text": chunk_text,
            "metadata": {
                "page_id": page_id,
                "page_title": title,
                "chunk_index": i
            }
        })

    store_chunks(chunks, namespace=namespace)
    print(f"Synced '{title}' → {len(chunks)} chunks stored")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("Starting sync...")
    page_id = os.getenv("NOTION_PAGE_ID")
    print(f"Page ID: {page_id}")
    sync_page_to_pinecone(page_id)
    print("Sync complete.")

---------------- FILE: backend/main.py ----------------
import os
import httpx
from fastapi import FastAPI, Request
from pydantic import BaseModel
from dotenv import load_dotenv
import json
import asyncio
import functools
load_dotenv()

app = FastAPI()


def build_transfer_sip_uri() -> str | None:
    """
    Build transfer SIP URI from environment variables.

    Priority:
    1. TRANSFER_SIP_URI (full URI, recommended)
    2. OWNER_PHONE + TRANSFER_SIP_DOMAIN
    """
    explicit_uri = os.getenv("TRANSFER_SIP_URI")
    if explicit_uri:
        return explicit_uri

    owner_phone = os.getenv("OWNER_PHONE")
    sip_domain = os.getenv("TRANSFER_SIP_DOMAIN")

    if owner_phone and sip_domain:
        return f"sip:{owner_phone}@{sip_domain}"

    return None

# ─── IN-MEMORY CALL STATE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
call_sessions = {}
owner_to_customer = {}


# ─── TENANT CONFIG ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# One tenant hardcoded for prototype.
# Later: fetch from Firebase by business_id.
# voice_system_prompt = exactly what owner writes in dashboard.

# Function Call Rules

You have access to the following tools.

### search_knowledge_base

Use this tool **if the customer asks something not covered in the business knowledge above**.

Example:

* product details
* special requests
* unusual event types

**If KB search returns no results:**

Say: "Let me get our team's direct contact for that question — would a callback be helpful?"

**If KB search fails or times out:**

Say: "I don't have that detail on hand, but I'll make sure the team can help when we talk. Is there anything else?"

Call:

search_knowledge_base(query)

---

### notify_owner

Call this tool when the customer:

• clearly wants to book
• asks to speak to the owner
• shows strong interest
• asks about immediate availability
• mentions urgency
• asks to confirm booking

When calling notify_owner, pass:

* customer_name
* call_summary
* reason_for_flagging

Example summary:

"Parent wants birthday party activity for around fifteen kids next Saturday evening at Whitefield."

After calling notify_owner say:

"Let me check availability with our team. Please hold for just a moment."

Then remain silent until instruction arrives.

---

### transfer_call_tool

If the system confirms the owner is available:

Say:

Then call:

---

### end_call_tool

If the owner is unavailable:

Say:

"Our team is a little occupied at the moment but they will call you back shortly. Thank you so much for your interest in Troy Blocks!"

Then call:

end_call_tool()

---

# Voice Behavior Rules

## Speech Normalization

Speak numbers naturally.

Examples:

399 → three hundred ninety nine
499 → four hundred ninety nine
3990 → three thousand nine hundred ninety

Do not say:

* "Rs"
* "rupees"
* digits individually

---

# Phone Number Rules

Phone numbers must be spoken **digit by digit**.

Example:

"nine eight seven, six five four, three two one zero"

Never add country code.

---

# Turn Discipline

• Ask **one question at a time**
• **Wait 2 seconds for response**
• If no response after 2 seconds: **repeat the question once, softly** (e.g., "Sorry, did you have a chance to think about that?")
• If **still no response** after second ask: **assume "no" or offer callback** ("No worries, we can call you back!")
• If caller says "one moment", **wait silently for 5 seconds**, then gently: "Still here whenever you're ready."
• Never ask same question 3+ times in a row

---

# Identity Rule

If asked who you are:

"I'm a virtual assistant helping coordinate Troy activity bookings."

If asked if you are AI:

"Yes, I'm a virtual assistant helping with booking coordination."

Keep explanations short.

---

# Silence Handling

**If customer goes silent > 3 seconds:**

Say: "I'm still here. Are you there?" or "Hello?"

**If silence continues > 2 more seconds:**

Say: "It seems like we lost the connection. No worries — we'll call you back!"

Then call end_call_tool().

---

# Closing

When ending the conversation:

"Thank you for your interest in Troy activities. Have a wonderful day.""",
    }
}

ACTIVE_TENANT_ID = "exnnpDvj3CUqdKdZb6SBNQM9gld2"


def get_tenant():
    return TENANT_CONFIG[ACTIVE_TENANT_ID]


# ─── VAPI HELPERS ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

async def make_vapi_call(
    assistant_id: str,
    phone: str,
    name: str,
    system_prompt: str,
    first_message: str,
    transfer_number: str | None = None
):
    """
    Fire an outbound VAPI call.
    Injects system_prompt + first_message via assistantOverrides.
    Optionally injects transfer destination for transfer_call_tool.
    """
    url = "https://api.vapi.ai/call"
    headers = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.getenv('VAPI_API_KEY')}",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    }

    assistant_overrides = {
        "firstMessage": first_message,
        "model": {
            "provider":"openai",
             "model": "gpt-4o-mini",
            "messages": [
                {
                    "role": "system",
                    "content": system_prompt
                }
            ]
        }
    }

    # Inject transfer destination if provided
    if transfer_number:
       assistant_overrides["tools:append"] = [
        {
            "type": "transferCall",
            "function":{
                "name":"transfer_call_tool",
                "description":"Transfer the customer call to the business owner. Only call this when explicitly instructed after owner confirms availability."
            },
            "destinations": [
                {
                    "type": "sip",
                    "sipUri": transfer_number,
                    "description": "Transfer to business owner"
                }
            ]
        }
    ]

    payload = {
        "assistantId": assistant_id,
        "phoneNumberId": os.getenv("VAPI_PHONE_NUMBER_ID"),
        "customer": {
            "number": phone,
            "name": name
        },
        "assistantOverrides": assistant_overrides
    }

    async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:
        resp = await client.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload)
    result = resp.json()
    print(f"VAPI call response ({resp.status_code}): {result}")
    return result

'''
async def send_background_message(customer_call_id: str, message: str):
    """
    Injects a system message into Ananya's active call mid-conversation.
    Used to tell Ananya to transfer or wrap up after owner decision.
    """
    session = call_sessions.get(customer_call_id, {})
    url = session.get("control_url")
    if not url:
       print(f"No control URL found for call {customer_call_id}")
    return
    headers = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.getenv('VAPI_API_KEY')}",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"

    payload = {
        "type": "add-message",
        "message": {
            "role": "system",
            "content": message
        }
    }
    async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:
        resp = await client.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload)
    print(f"Background message response: {resp.status_code} {resp.text}")
    return resp
'''
async def send_background_message(customer_call_id: str, message: str):
    """
    Injects a system message into Ananya's active call mid-conversation.
    Used to tell Ananya to transfer or wrap up after owner decision.
    """
    session = call_sessions.get(customer_call_id, {})
    url = session.get("control_url")

    if not url:
        print(f"No control URL found for call {customer_call_id}")
        return # Correctly placed inside the if-block

    headers = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.getenv('VAPI_API_KEY')}",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    }
    payload = {
        "type": "add-message",
        "message": {
            "role": "system",
            "content": message
        }
    }

    async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:
        # VAPI Control API uses POST to the monitor.controlUrl
        resp = await client.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload)

    print(f"Background message response: {resp.status_code} {resp.text}")
    return resp


async def command_customer_call(customer_call_id: str, decision: str):
    tenant = get_tenant()

    if decision == "yes":
        session = call_sessions.get(customer_call_id, {})
        control_url = session.get("control_url")

        if control_url:
            # Tell Ananya to say the handoff line
            await send_background_message(
                customer_call_id,
                "The owner is available. Say exactly: 'Great news! The owner is ready to speak with you. Connecting you now, please hold.' then stop speaking."
            )

            # Small delay to let Ananya finish speaking
            import asyncio
            await asyncio.sleep(4)

            # Execute the transfer directly from backend via controlUrl
            headers = {
                "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.getenv('VAPI_API_KEY')}",
                "Content-Type": "application/json"
            }
            transfer_payload = {
                "type": "transfer",
                "destination": {
                    "type": "sip",
                    "sipUri": tenant["transfer_sip_uri"]
                }
            }
            async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:
                resp = await client.post(control_url, headers=headers, json=transfer_payload)
            print(f"Transfer via controlUrl: {resp.status_code} {resp.text}")

        else:
            print(f"No control URL for call {customer_call_id}, cannot transfer")

    elif decision == "no":
        await send_background_message(
            customer_call_id,
            f"The owner is currently unavailable. "
            f"Say 'I'm sorry, our team at {tenant['business_name']} is a little occupied "
            f"at the moment. They will call you back shortly. Thank you so much!' then call end_call_tool."
        )

    elif decision == "voicemail":
        await send_background_message(
            customer_call_id,
            f"The owner did not pick up. "
            f"Say 'Our team seems to be unavailable right now but will call you back soon. "
            f"Thank you for your interest in {tenant['business_name']}!' then call end_call_tool."
        )




# ─── ROUTES ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

class CallbackRequest(BaseModel):
    name: str
    phone: str
    conversation_summary: str


@app.post("/trigger-call")
async def trigger_call(req: CallbackRequest):
    """
    Called by Streamlit frontend when customer requests callback.
    Fires Ananya call with full prompt + transfer destination injected.
    """
    tenant = get_tenant()

    if not tenant.get("transfer_sip_uri"):
        raise ValueError(
            "Transfer SIP destination is not configured. Set TRANSFER_SIP_URI or both OWNER_PHONE and TRANSFER_SIP_DOMAIN in .env"
        )

    # Full system prompt = base voice prompt + chat summary appended
    full_system_prompt = (
        tenant["voice_system_prompt"]
        + f"\n\n---\nChat Context (prior conversation with customer):\n{req.conversation_summary}"
    )

    # First message with customer name substituted
    first_message = tenant["voice_welcome_message"].replace(
        "{customer_name}", req.name
    )

    assistant_id = os.getenv("VAPI_ASSISTANT_ID")
    if not assistant_id:
        raise ValueError("VAPI_ASSISTANT_ID environment variable is not set")

    result = await make_vapi_call(
        assistant_id=assistant_id,
        phone=req.phone,
        name=req.name,
        system_prompt=full_system_prompt,
        first_message=first_message,
        transfer_number=tenant["transfer_sip_uri"],
    )

    call_id = result.get("id")
    if call_id:
        call_sessions[call_id] = {
            "customer_name": req.name,
            "customer_phone": req.phone,
            "conversation_summary": req.conversation_summary,
            "owner_call_triggered": False,
            "owner_call_id": None,
            "control_url": result.get("monitor", {}).get("controlUrl"),
        }
        print(f"Customer call triggered: {call_id}")

    return {"status": "call initiated", "call_id": call_id}


@app.post("/notify-owner")
async def notify_owner(request: Request):
    """
    Called by Ananya's notify_owner tool when she detects a high lead.
    Receives: customer_name, call_summary, lead_reason
    Fires Owner PA call with full context injected.
    """
    data = await request.json()
    print(f"notify_owner called: {data}")

    tool_call_id = data.get("message", {}).get("toolCallList", [{}])[0].get("id")
    arguments = data.get("message", {}).get("toolCallList", [{}])[0].get("function", {}).get("arguments", {})
    customer_name = arguments.get("customer_name", "the customer")
    call_summary = arguments.get("call_summary", "")
    lead_reason = arguments.get("lead_reason", "")
    customer_call_id = data.get("message", {}).get("call", {}).get("id")

    print(f"Customer: {customer_name}")
    print(f"Summary: {call_summary}")
    print(f"Reason: {lead_reason}")

    tenant = get_tenant()

    # Build Owner PA prompt with full customer context injected
    pa_system_prompt = f"""[Identity]
You are a professional, efficient AI assistant representing SuperOwl.
Your role is to inform the {tenant['business_name']} owner about a qualified lead
and get their availability decision quickly.

[Style]
- Concise, clear, and professional.
- No small talk. Stay focused.
- Sound human — use brief natural pauses.


[Customer Context]
Customer Name: {customer_name}
What they want: {call_summary}
Quality indicator: {lead_reason}

[Task]
1. Say: "Hello {tenant['owner_name']}, this is SuperOwl calling to inform of a lead. I have a qualified customer on the line."
2. Brief the owner: "{customer_name} wants to {call_summary}."
3. Ask: "Are you available to speak with them right now?"
4. Wait for response.
5. If YES: Say "Perfect, connecting you now." → call report_decision with decision="yes" → end call.
6. If NO: Say "No problem, I will let them know. Thank you!" → call report_decision with decision="no" → end call.
7. If no clear answer: ask once more. If still unclear → assume "no" → call report_decision with decision="no" → end call.

[Critical Rule]
Always call report_decision before ending.
Decision must be "yes" or "no" only. Nothing else."""

    pa_first_message = (
        f"Hello {tenant['owner_name']}, am I speaking to the owner of {tenant['business_name']}?"
    )

    owner_assistant_id = os.getenv("VAPI_OWNER_ASSISTANT_ID")
    if not owner_assistant_id:
        raise ValueError("VAPI_OWNER_ASSISTANT_ID environment variable is not set")

    # Fire Owner PA call
    owner_result = await make_vapi_call(
        assistant_id=owner_assistant_id,
        phone=tenant["owner_phone"],
        name=tenant["owner_name"],
        system_prompt=pa_system_prompt,
        first_message=pa_first_message,
    )

    owner_call_id = owner_result.get("id")
    if owner_call_id and customer_call_id:
        owner_to_customer[owner_call_id] = customer_call_id
        if customer_call_id in call_sessions:
            call_sessions[customer_call_id]["owner_call_triggered"] = True
            call_sessions[customer_call_id]["owner_call_id"] = owner_call_id
        print(f"Owner PA call triggered: {owner_call_id} → customer: {customer_call_id}")

    return {
        "results": [
            {
                "toolCallId": tool_call_id,
                "result": "Owner has been notified. Please hold while we check availability."
            }
        ]
    }


@app.post("/owner-decision")
async def owner_decision(request: Request):
    """
    Called by Owner PA's report_decision tool.
    Receives owner's yes/no/voicemail decision.
    Commands Ananya via background message injection.
    """
    data = await request.json()
    print(f"Owner decision received: {data}")

    tool_call_id = data.get("message", {}).get("toolCallList", [{}])[0].get("id")
    arguments = data.get("message", {}).get("toolCallList", [{}])[0].get("function", {}).get("arguments", {})
    decision = arguments.get("decision", "").lower()
    owner_call_id = data.get("message", {}).get("call", {}).get("id")

    print(f"Decision: {decision}, owner_call_id: {owner_call_id}")

    customer_call_id = owner_to_customer.get(owner_call_id)

    if customer_call_id:
        print(f"Commanding customer call: {customer_call_id} with decision: {decision}")
        await command_customer_call(customer_call_id, decision)
    else:
        print(f"No customer call found for owner call: {owner_call_id}")

    messages = {
        "yes": "Transfer initiated. Customer is being connected to the owner now.",
        "no": "Noted. Customer has been informed the team will call back shortly.",
    }

    return {
        "results": [
            {
                "toolCallId": tool_call_id,
                "result": messages.get(decision, "Decision recorded.")
            }
        ]
    }


@app.post("/vapi-webhook")
async def vapi_webhook(request: Request):
    """
    Receives all VAPI call events.
    Used for logging and call state tracking only.
    Qualification detection removed — Ananya decides via notify_owner tool.
    """
    data = await request.json()
    event_type = data.get("message", {}).get("type")
    call_id = data.get("message", {}).get("call", {}).get("id")

    print(f"VAPI webhook: {event_type} | call_id: {call_id}")

    if event_type == "call-ended":
        if call_id in call_sessions:
            print(f"Call ended. Session: {call_sessions[call_id]}")
        elif call_id in owner_to_customer.values():
            print(f"Owner PA call ended.")
    #this is for the summary
    if event_type == "end-of-call-report":
        msg = data.get("message", {})
        customer_name = msg.get("call", {}).get("customer", {}).get("name", "Unknown")
        customer_phone = msg.get("call", {}).get("customer", {}).get("number", "Unknown")
        duration_s = int(msg.get("durationSeconds", 0))
        duration_str = f"{duration_s // 60}m {duration_s % 60}s"
        ended_reason = msg.get("endedReason", "unknown")
        transcript = msg.get("transcript", "No transcript available.")
        started_at = msg.get("startedAt", "")[:16].replace("T", " ")
        assistant_name = msg.get("assistant", {}).get("name", "")

        print(f"END OF CALL REPORT: {assistant_name} | {customer_name} | {duration_str} | {ended_reason}")
        if assistant_name == "ananya":
            slack_url = os.getenv("SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL")
            if slack_url:
                slack_msg = {
                    "text": (
                        f"🤖 Ananya Call Report\n"
                        f"Customer: {customer_name} ({customer_phone})\n"
                        f"Duration: {duration_str}\n"
                        f"Reason: {ended_reason}\n"
                        f"Time: {started_at}\n\n"
                        f"Transcript:\n```\n{transcript}\n```"
                    )
                }
                def send_slack():
                    import httpx
                    r = httpx.post(slack_url, json=slack_msg, timeout=15.0,verify=False)
                    return r.status_code, r.text

                try:
                    loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
                    status, text = await loop.run_in_executor(None, send_slack)
                    print(f"Slack response: {status} {text}")
                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"Slack notification failed (non-fatal): {type(e).__name__}: {repr(e)}")
    return {"status": "ok"}


@app.post("/query-kb")
async def query_kb(request: Request):
    """
    Called by Ananya's search_knowledge_base tool during voice calls.
    Searches Pinecone and returns relevant KB chunks.
    """
    data = await request.json()

    tool_call_id = data.get("message", {}).get("toolCallList", [{}])[0].get("id", "")
    arguments = data.get("message", {}).get("toolCallList", [{}])[0].get("function", {}).get("arguments", {})
    query = arguments.get("query", "")

    if not query:
        query = data.get("query", "")

    print(f"KB query: {query}")

    tenant = get_tenant()

    from kb.embeddings import search_chunks
    chunks = search_chunks(query=query, namespace=tenant["kb_namespace"], top_k=3)
    context = "\n".join([c["text"] for c in chunks])

    print(f"KB result preview: {context[:200]}")

    if tool_call_id:
        return {
            "results": [
                {
                    "toolCallId": tool_call_id,
                    "result": context
                }
            ]
        }

    return {"result": context}

Replace outbound direct Slack calls with Nango proxy.

Build Slack Block Kit buttons (live call: Whisper, Take Over, Transfer, End; post-call: Full Transcript, Call Back, Mark Resolved).

Wire HTML dashboard to real backend endpoints (/businesses, /trigger-call, /slack/action, etc.).

Package with .env.example, README.md, and demo script.


===== main.py =====
"""SuperOwl Voice AI POC — Main Application Entry Point."""

from contextlib import asynccontextmanager

from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.responses import FileResponse
from fastapi.staticfiles import StaticFiles
import pathlib

from app.routers import (
    businesses,
    onboarding,
    playground,
    prompts,
    slack_actions,
    slack_events,
    trigger,
    vapi_webhook,
)


@asynccontextmanager
async def lifespan(app: FastAPI):
    """Startup and shutdown events."""
    # No database setup needed — using JSON file storage
    yield


app = FastAPI(
    title="SuperOwl Voice AI",
    description="Multi‑tenant voice AI platform for inbound/outbound calls",
    version="0.1.0",
    lifespan=lifespan,
)

# CORS for frontend
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],  # Restrict in production
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# Include routers
app.include_router(businesses.router, prefix="/businesses", tags=["Businesses"])
app.include_router(prompts.router, prefix="/prompts", tags=["Prompts"])
app.include_router(trigger.router, prefix="/trigger", tags=["Call Triggers"])
app.include_router(vapi_webhook.router, prefix="/vapi-webhook", tags=["VAPI Webhooks"])
# Note: /vapi-webhook/notify-owner and /vapi-webhook/owner-decision are handled by the same router

# Dual-agent endpoints (must be at root level for VAPI tool calls)
from app.routers.vapi_webhook import notify_owner, owner_decision
app.add_api_route("/notify-owner", notify_owner, methods=["POST"], tags=["Dual Agent"])
app.add_api_route("/owner-decision", owner_decision, methods=["POST"], tags=["Dual Agent"])

app.include_router(slack_events.router, prefix="/slack/events", tags=["Slack Events"])
app.include_router(
    slack_actions.router, prefix="/slack/actions", tags=["Slack Actions"]
)
app.include_router(onboarding.router, prefix="/onboarding", tags=["Onboarding"])
app.include_router(playground.router, prefix="/playground", tags=["Playground"])


# Frontend static files
FRONTEND_DIR = pathlib.Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "frontend"
app.mount("/static", StaticFiles(directory=str(FRONTEND_DIR)), name="static")


@app.get("/")
async def serve_frontend():
    """Serve the Voice Configuration dashboard."""
    return FileResponse(str(FRONTEND_DIR / "index.html"))


@app.get("/health")
async def health_check():
    return {"status": "healthy"}


if __name__ == "__main__":
    import uvicorn

    uvicorn.run("main:app", host="0.0.0.0", port=8000, reload=True)

    <div style="background:#fafbff;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;padding:13px 18px;margin-bottom:16px;display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:14px">
      <span style="font-size:20px;flex-shrink:0">🔀</span>
      <div style="font-size:12.5px;color:var(--text-2);line-height:1.65">
        <strong style="color:var(--text)">How this works:</strong> Each business owner configures call forwarding on their own phone number to your shared SuperOwl DID <code style="background:var(--bg);padding:2px 7px;border-radius:4px;font-family:'DM Mono',monospace;font-size:12px">+91 80 4568 XXXX</code>. When a customer calls the business, their phone forwards it. Vapi reads the <strong>SIP Diversion header</strong> to know which business it is, then loads that business's personalised AI agent automatically.
      </div>

    <!-- Loop detection notice -->
    <div style="background:#fff7ed;border:1.5px solid var(--orange);border-radius:10px;padding:12px 18px;margin-bottom:16px;display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:12px">
      <span style="font-size:18px;flex-shrink:0">🔁</span>
      <div style="font-size:12.5px;color:#7c2d12;line-height:1.65">
        <strong>Outbound → Inbound loop detection is active.</strong> If SuperOwl places an outbound callback and the business owner's phone forwards it back to the SuperOwl DID (because they're busy), the system detects the loop, marks the owner as <em>busy</em>, and instructs the outbound AI agent to inform the customer: <em>"The team is currently with another customer — I'll make sure someone follows up with you shortly."</em>
      </div>
    </div>
